Many Insane People in Shanghai

Insanity is one of the diseases of civilization. The more advanced and complex society becomes, the more frequently this disease is found. It is also related to the climate. Since the beginning of summer in Shanghai, various police stations have repeatedly detained insane people on the streets and sent them to the Shanghai Mental Hospital affiliated with the China Mental Hospital next to the Dong Youheng Road vegetable market in Hongkou for treatment. It is said that the hospital is large-scale and the treatment is rapid. It is estimated that those admitted to the hospital for treatment this week include Zhao Zhennan from Shaoxing, Ni Tingxiang from the Qiashengchang store on Zhoujiazui Road in Hongkou, and Chen Lu from the Sanyixin Silk Weaving Factory on Zhoujiazui Road. In addition, there are also an unknown female madwoman detained by the Hongkou police station, Yang Aquan, Yu Ren detained by the Jing'an Temple police station, an unknown madwoman detained by the Jiaxing Road police station, and Wu Yuankang detained by the Laozha police station, totaling 17 people. Among them, Yang Aquan, sent by the Hongkou police station, and Yu Ren, sent by the Jing'an Temple police station, are said to have been cured and discharged from the hospital after only five or six days of treatment.

Minutes of the National Lixue (Rational Learning) Association Meeting

The China National Lixue Federation held its 46th meeting the day before yesterday, chaired by Zhang Yichen. The discussion included: (1) A letter from the County Party Department of Shoufeng County, Anhui, regarding the approval of the Zhishiwutang Public Office, etc., for separate filing and a public letter to the county government for protection. It was resolved to forward the letter to the public office. (2) A letter from the Chengshantang Public Office in Haiyang, Shandong, requesting the issuance of a notice and certificate from the association for protection. It was resolved to refer it to the investigation department. (3) A letter from the Gaoyou Lixue Federation in Jiangsu, regarding how to handle a part of the public offices in the county that have similar organizations. It was resolved to reply that two associations cannot be organized in one county. (4) A letter from the Tongxiutang Public Office in Weixian County, Hebei, stating that the public office's documents and deeds were scattered and lost due to the rebellion by Liu Guitang's troops, but work has been restored and officials have been re-elected, requesting filing. It was resolved to approve and send a public letter to the Weixian County Government. (5) A letter from the Shenshentang Public Office in Xinghua, Jiangsu, stating that the public office's premises were occupied by county police, hindering work, and requesting intervention. It was resolved to reply, requesting a detailed report of the situation for further review. (6) A letter from the Lixue Federation in Lingbi, Anhui, stating that the membership of the Guzhen Shenshentang Public Office was unclear and requesting the original case. It was resolved to refer it to the review department. (7) A letter from the Tongshentang Public Office in Shaanxi County, Henan, requesting a request to the authorities for protection. It was resolved to forward the request. (8) A letter from the Lishentang Public Office in Huixian County, Gansu, stating that the county government has been requested to give a protective notice, which has been received and hung, and requesting the issuance of a picture certificate. It was resolved to refer it to the organization department for handling. (9) A letter from the Lixue Federation in Suxian County, Anhui, stating that it has been filed with the party and government organs, has been formally established, and officials have been elected, requesting filing. It was resolved to approve. (10) Cases in which the Lixue public offices stationed in the United Kingdom, Russia, and North Korea have not reported their work for a long time. It was resolved to send letters to the directors of each public office, requesting them to report within the prescribed time limit. The rest is omitted.

Letter

To the Editor: I recently read a news report on the fourth page of today's newspaper entitled "Disabled Anti-Japanese Soldiers Request Relief." The report stated that Yao Ziyu and others were originally from the Northeast and followed Mr. Ma in fighting the Japanese. They were injured and disabled and came to Shanghai to visit Mr. Ma, but he happened to be in Lushan for summer vacation. Recently, they repeatedly visited me, but I refused to see them. I am shocked to read this. Although I am in Shanghai, I am fulfilling my responsibility to speak out for my fellow Northeasterners. It is driven by my personal conscience and I am not responsible for anyone, nor have I been entrusted by Mr. Ma to be in charge of affairs in Shanghai. As for Yao and the other seven people, they have never met me, so it is incomprehensible to say that they visited me and were refused. However, I would like to state that even if the seven people met me, it would only be to no avail. We are fellow sufferers. Because we are all people from the lost province, displaced and unable to take care of ourselves. I am deeply afraid that the rumors are untrue. I hope that your newspaper will correct them in the letter column. Sincerely, Wu Huanzhang, August 8.

Spring and Autumn

The Misty Records of Imperial Incense

— Original work by Princess Der Ling of Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Behind this throne, as usual, there was inevitably a screen. Its material was also rosewood, lacquered very brightly, and inlaid with invaluable jade and gemstones. However, no one could say what its real use was. It was only known that it was always connected to the throne. Wherever there was a throne, there must be a screen behind it; wherever there was a screen, there must be a throne in front of it. These two things had simply become an inseparable set of furniture. It is said that this custom has been followed for generations, not only in the Qing Palace. Unfortunately, no one can say how this special custom was created in the first place!

I just said that the screen behind the throne, no one knows what its real use is, but on the train, it shows part of its effect. The Empress Dowager usually takes a nap often, so we specially prepared a small soft couch for her, placed behind this screen, so that she can rest at any time during the day, and there is no need to return to that small bedroom specifically.

I remember very clearly that when our journey had just begun, at the Yongdingmen Station, the Empress Dowager, supported by me and a few others, stepped onto this novel means of transportation for the first time, she initially seemed a bit embarrassed; because although the layout of this carriage and bedroom had undergone the design and efforts of many people, it was more mysterious than all the great halls and bedrooms in the palace, and it could be praised as "ingenious and unique," but their area was ultimately limited by the position of the train. No matter which great engineer was consulted, it was probably impossible to expand it. And the Empress Dowager was accustomed to spacious and grand places in the past. Once suddenly placed in such a narrow room, she would naturally feel a bit different in spirit. However, after five or six minutes, she gradually got used to it. The first thing she said was to order those eunuchs to check clearly whether the direction of her throne was indeed the same as the direction of the train's advancement, because she felt that if she turned her back and let the train drag her, always going backwards, it would be very detrimental to her dignity. (101)

Summer Nights

— Yan Qiao

In the poet's pen, the loveliness of summer nights is often written, especially with a hint of sexual atmosphere. It is true that we can easily find this kind of material when we go to the city. Not to mention the dance halls and bathhouses in Shanghai, and all the places with romantic sentiments, Suzhou's parks alone are enough to write a magnificent masterpiece.

But, how do other summer nights pass? Apart from sleeping in the streets, there is only the option of squeezing into pigeon cages that are like fire pits. Fortunately, there are particularly few mosquitoes and insects this year, probably because of the long drought, their reproductive capacity has also decreased. Indeed, the situation is very serious. We haven't heard people singing folk songs on the streets to attract people to enjoy the cool air for a long time. This can prove that they have no interest in appreciating and praising this summer night anymore. What we often hear is the sound of various different buckets hitting the stone well railing at the public well outside the door, almost rhythmically. We can't help but look up at the sky, resenting those twinkling stars, always staring wide-eyed, is it possible that this year's summer night will always be so dry that even dew cannot form?

Summer nights in the city are, in any case, a little better than in the countryside. A few days ago, it wasn't as dry or as hot as it is now, but when I passed through the countryside, looking from the boat to the shore, the young crops looked withered and about to die. Dogs stick out their two or three-inch-long red tongues. Children immerse themselves in the shallow water of the shore. Although the setting sun had already gone down, and the twilight had gradually deepened, everything was still in distress, without any sign of recovery. It can be said that predicting their fate this year, I can't help but feel cold for them; even if we think about ourselves, we won't have time to grieve for ourselves.

The "Chinese Daily News" is Shenbao's Elder Brother

— Jing Feifeng

I read Mr. Yan Qiao's article "Shenbao's Elder Brother" before, which said that there is also a "Circulation Daily News" in Hong Kong, which held its 70th anniversary last year... Then it is nine years older than Shenbao, and should be called the eldest brother.... However, the author happened to borrow a copy of Chinese Journalism published by Modern Book Company (written by Huang Tianpeng, published by Hong Kong Dianfan) from the circulation library attached to the Shenbao office yesterday, which included an appendix "Chronicle of Major Events in the News Industry in the Last Hundred Years," which stated "In 1872 AD (i.e., the 11th year of Tongzhi), Shenbao was published in Shanghai, initially run by the British man Meizha, and later taken over by Mr. Xi. After the Republic of China, it belonged to Mr. Shi Liangcai, and with its long history, it led the country." "In 1873 AD (i.e., the 12th year of Tongzhi), Zhaowen Xinbao was founded in Hankou, advocated by Ai Xiaomei, as the first newspaper run by the Chinese themselves," "In 1874 AD (i.e., the 13th year of Tongzhi), Circulation Daily News was published, by Wang Tao and Wang Gan, and still exists independently in Hong Kong." From this point of view, although the "Circulation Daily News" in Hong Kong has a long history since its publication, it was not published as early as Shenbao (less than three years difference), then Shenbao is still the "Circulation Daily News"'s elder brother. According to another record, "In 1864 AD (i.e., the 3rd year of Tongzhi), Chinese Daily News was published, hosted by Chen Aiting, initially a Chinese newspaper of the German Chenbao, with only a quarter of the current size, and mainly translated Western newspapers and reprinted the Beijing Gazette, and still exists in Hong Kong, as one of the oldest Chinese newspapers." According to this, Shenbao's elder brother is actually the "Chinese Daily News," because the "Chinese Daily News" was published nine years earlier than Shenbao.

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Thirty-Two: The General Amuses Himself with Sensual Pleasures All Day Long; Several Crying Soldiers Return

After about ten minutes, the old lady came out, not walking on her own, but being supported by a servant. The old lady's face was full of tears, trembling, with her mouth open and unable to close it. The servant kept telling her not to cry, and helped her out all the way. Another servant led Mrs. Guan in. Seeing this scene, Guizhi was already flustered, not knowing what to do, just sitting there blankly. After another ten minutes or so, Mrs. Guan came stumbling out with a child in her arms, followed by two children. She couldn't follow the rules like the old lady, and had already cried out loud. She counted her grievances: "Oh my god, leaving these three children to me, what am I going to do?" Guizhi rushed forward, blocking her and asking: "Sister-in-law, what... what's wrong?" Mrs. Guan said with tears: "Company Commander Yin said that he didn't die when he jumped down the city, he slept in a hole for a day, and crawled out in the dark before being rescued. Only a dozen brothers from the whole battalion came back, he saw with his own eyes... what am I going to do?" Several servants crowded forward, not allowing her to cry anymore, quickly pushing and persuading her out. At this time, Guizhi was really flustered. Thinking that if she went in and asked Company Commander Yin, there was no doubt that she would also cry. If she didn't go in and ask him, she wouldn't know what was going on with her husband. Struggling like this, she started crying first. At this moment, there was a servant who was about to lead him in to see the patient, but seeing that he hadn't gone in and was crying first, he stood there in a daze for a long time before asking: "Aren't you going in to see him?" Guizhi wiped her eyes and said: "I'm afraid that if I go in, he'll tell me bad news." The servant didn't understand what she meant, and couldn't wait any longer, so he turned around and left on his own. Guizhi wanted to follow him in, but it was too late, she had no idea, and had to go to the reception room. She saw the old lady Tian, Mrs. Guan, and those children crying together outside the door. She didn't go forward, and didn't know where the grief came from, so she just watched from afar and started crying too. The receptionist, who was about fifty years old, was a kind-hearted person, and greeted Guizhi: "Madam, have you seen the news about your company commander?" Guizhi said: "No, I saw one going in and one coming out crying, and I didn't dare to ask Company Commander Yin." The receptionist said: "Nonsense! Why didn't you go in? How can you find out if you don't go in? Come with me." So he led Guizhi forward again. (452)

Miscellaneous Remarks

Gem Among Men (Part 1)

— Tianxu Wosheng

The Spring and Autumn issue of July 23rd of the 23rd year [of the Republic, i.e., 1934] contained a telegram from Mr. Wang Shouqiu about a "human gem." The object described therein was most likely a child's toy swallowed by a turtle, certainly not naturally formed, because the "ma bao" (horse gem) type of object is always a mineral concretion. In the third year of the Republic [1914], I personally witnessed one dissected from the belly of a horse in Huai'an. It was as large as a goose egg, wrapped in a thin membrane, with many bluish-purple, red, and yellow veins visible inside. It was as hard as stone, weighing about two liang (approximately 74 grams), and was priced at 800 yuan. It was ultimately purchased by a druggist. I obtained one qian (approximately 3.7 grams) for 20 yuan, and when tested with tri-acid, it did not react, possessing the same properties as talc. Generally, this is due to the ingestion of substances containing magnesium salts and silicic acid, similar to how gravel accumulates in the bladder, but in this case, it accumulates in the stomach. Cancer of the stomach in humans is exactly analogous to this. Volume 52 of the Compendium of Materia Medica, in the section on humans, contains an entry on "bi shi" (stone concretion), detailing its composition in great detail. Descriptions of human-shaped objects refer to the mottled patterns on the cross-section, similar to the veining of marble, able to form landscapes and figures, not an entire form. Mr. Wang likely did not witness it firsthand, and thus propagated an error. These concretions have their own names, such as "niu huang zha da" (ox gall residue), all of which are "ma bao" types of objects. In humans, it is called "bi shi," not "bao" (gem), because dogs and horses are inherently base creatures. Obtaining such an object gives them extraordinary value, and thus it is considered a "gem." If humans possess it, it leads to illness and death; what "gem" is that? In general, when people are particularly fond of something, it is called a "pi" (addiction). The deeper the "pi," the more one's spirit concentrates on it, and thus the heart's blood coagulates and transforms into a stone-like substance. Therefore, the corpses described by Li Shizhen all had "bi shi" in the heart chamber, which is different from those caused by diet. "Ma bao" is a magical medicine for treating madness, but it must be supplemented with phlegm-resolving ingredients to have a miraculous effect. Its significance lies in the mutual induction of similar things, thus it is used as a guiding agent. When horses suffer from madness, dissecting them will inevitably yield a "ma bao." In Huai'an, one or two can be obtained every year. Generally, Huai salt contains a large amount of magnesium. If a horse drinks water containing sodium silicate, it will combine to form magnesium silicate stone, leading to a feeling of obstruction, and thus madness. Traditional Chinese medicine uses drugs, all taking similar types as guiding agents, which is consistent with chemical principles. Using "ma bao" to treat human blockages is because human "pi shi" cannot be obtained. Living "ma bao" must be obtained from living animals. In the past, there was no dissection of living humans to obtain human "bi shi," thus it is not found in the world. The "bi shi" recorded in the Compendium of Materia Medica only refers to those obtained from corpses, not from living creatures. Living "ma bao" must be obtained from living animals, and is called "living gem" by the world, extremely emphasizing its rarity. However, my family actually has what Mr. Wang idealizes as a "human gem," which is also sufficient for conversation. For details, see the preface to my work Half-Acre Garden, dedicated to the French doctor Xie Bi, which says, "My second daughter-in-law suffered from a severe 'river fish' disease (ectopic pregnancy). Various doctors gave different opinions, without any consensus. Each attack caused unbearable pain. In April of gengwu year [1930], an attack did not stop. Treatment continued for ten days, but worsened. Only when Dr. Xie Bi was consulted and diagnosed it as an ectopic pregnancy, which could only be cured by surgery. Initially, we dared not try, but when it became unavoidable, the abdomen was opened, and a huge object like a fist was extracted, half a foot long, nearly one foot in circumference, and weighing about two pounds. Its outer shape resembled a sac, and its inner part was hard, suspected to be bone. When it was cut into three pieces, it turned out to be completely stone, similar to 'ma bao.' Examining the Compendium of Materia Medica, it is called 'bi shi.' Since ancient times, no one has obtained it from the abdomen of a living person. It is said to be able to treat hernias, so we preserved it."

Education News

The Enslavement Education in the Northeast is Gradually Taking Concrete Shape

All Kinds of Measures Come from Japanese Instigation

To Eliminate Our National Character in Order to Achieve Assimilation

(Northeast News Agency, Shenyang) The budget of the puppet "Ministry of Education" for this year, including the regular and temporary sections, totals 6,114,268 yuan, an increase of more than six times compared to the previous year's budget of 930,000 yuan (including supplementary budgets). The main undertakings planned by the puppet Ministry of Education in the new year's budget are listed below:

Higher Normal School: This school is the highest institution in the puppet organization and a training institution for secondary school teachers. The school site has been set up at the old site of Jilin University. The establishment cost is estimated at more than 300,000 yuan. A preparatory committee for the establishment of the school has now been set up within the puppet Ministry of Education, and preparations are being made step by step. It is scheduled to open in mid-August. The initial number of students enrolled in the first year is 150. The principal and all staff of the school are currently being selected by the puppet Ministry of Education, and no final decision has been made.

Agricultural Vocational School: Following the highest institution, the Higher Normal School, four vocational schools of agriculture, industry, commerce and medicine will be established. Below these are the so-called primary and secondary schools. The school system at all levels will be completed. In the new year, the Agricultural Vocational School will be established first, and it is planned to open in "Fengtian" in January next year. The initial number of students enrolled is planned to be 100.

Enhance Teacher Training: Enhance the current puppet Capital Teacher Training Institute, extend the training period of the former three-month training institute to six months, and implement matters such as training personnel and moving school buildings. In addition, it is also necessary to expand the local teacher training conferences at various sites.

Increase Tuition Fees for Studying in Japan: Advocate enslavement education and encourage studying in Japan. Many teachers and students in the Northeast are induced to study in Japan. Therefore, the subsidy for tuition fees for studying abroad is gradually increased. On the one hand, in order to liaise with the puppet Ministry of Foreign Affairs, a new puppet Study Abroad Affairs Office is added to the puppet embassy in Japan to handle affairs between the puppet Ministry of Education and the puppet students studying abroad.

Preservation of Ancient Sites and Relics: Preservation of ancient sites and relics throughout the puppet state is a point of particular attention for the Japanese side. It is planned to repair the Summer Palace Lama Pagoda in Rehe Province first, and establish a treasure house to preserve ancient relics for public viewing.

Implementation of Social Education: Social education will be carried out in parallel with school education. In the new year, film education, moral education, public education, and the enhancement of local museums and libraries will be implemented. This is the first year of the so-called five-year plan for social education. In addition, new budget items include 106 provincial special primary and secondary schools and cultural institutions such as provincial museums and libraries, which were previously under the budget of the Ministry of Civil Affairs, and have now been transferred to the puppet Ministry of Education. This expenditure amounts to more than 3.3 million yuan. In order to improve the quality of teachers in enslavement primary and secondary schools, a certification system must be established, which will be implemented starting this year. In addition, it is also planned to provide free textbooks for elementary schools and printed materials such as the Veritable Records of the Qing Dynasty. All these measures are instigated or ordered by the Japanese in order to form a situation of assimilation as soon as possible. At the same time, on the surface, it can also make the ignorant or short-sighted people sing praises and virtues, while eliminating our national character. The insidious cultural aggression of the violent Japanese is indeed beyond description.

Ministry of Education's Instruction for Vocational Schools and Above

Key Points for Improvement in Various Schools (8)

Hunan Provincial University

The school's environment is suitable for academic research. The departments and faculties established meet local needs. Most of the faculty and staff are able to diligently perform their duties. Students are diligent in their studies and abide by the rules. Enrollment is also relatively strict. However, the engineering building and exhibition hall of the Faculty of Engineering should be urgently constructed to establish a permanent foundation for the faculty and to inspire people's knowledge of science and practical technology. The equipment of each department is still too simple. Equipment fees should be increased in the future, focusing on enriching the content and then seeking the expansion of departments and faculties. The treatment of teachers should also be appropriately increased so as to attract experts from all parties.

Private Franco-Chinese University

The school has made considerable progress in recent years. However, there are still many areas that need to be improved. The key points are presented below:

(1) The name of the school's Faculty of Social Sciences is inconsistent with the University Organization Law. The Department of Philosophy and Department of Social Sciences established therein have many overlapping courses with the Department of Chinese Studies, Department of French Literature, and Department of Economics of the Faculty of Arts. The teachers also hold concurrent positions. The personnel in charge of the faculty cannot be in the faculty on a daily basis, and the faculty is far away from other faculties, making management difficult. In terms of economy, administration, and teaching, it is inconvenient. The faculty should be abolished immediately, and the original departments should be incorporated into the Faculty of Arts for management, or the students should be incorporated into the departments of the Faculty of Arts. The senior high school classes of the three divisions of the faculties and the Comte School can be moved into the remaining school buildings of the faculty and managed centrally.

(2) The names of the school's Fold College, Curie College, Lumo Ke College, and Comte College, used to replace the four faculties of Arts, Science, Medicine, and Social Sciences, are inconsistent with the regulations. Except for Comte College, which should be abolished immediately, Fold, Curie, and Lumo Ke Colleges should be renamed as Faculty of Arts, Faculty of Science, and Faculty of Medicine, respectively. The names that have been used for a long time originally have the meaning of commemorating famous scientists, and can be reserved for use as the names of the buildings of each faculty, such as Fold College and Curie College.

(3) The school's funding is limited. If other undertakings gradually increase, the development of the university part will be affected. In the future, the university's funding should be determined so that it can develop independently.

(4) The school's faculty and staff should be increased as much as possible on a full-time basis, and the treatment should be appropriately increased. The equipment should also be strengthened, and special attention should be paid to student training.

Private Wuchang Wenhua Library Science Vocational School

The school is run conscientiously, and the talents it cultivates are quite able to adapt to the needs of society, which is commendable. However, the school's own equipment is too simple and should be strengthened. The place for students to practice is only the library of Central China University, which does not have many books, and Chinese books are particularly lacking. Books should be purchased urgently, or ways should be found to expand internship opportunities to facilitate training.

Private Wuchang Art Vocational School

The key points for improvement in the school are specially presented as follows:

(1) The vocational and secondary school parts of the school should be managed separately as soon as possible.

(2) The school's curriculum teaching should focus on practicality and application to meet the needs of society. The curriculum outline should be compiled and submitted to the Ministry for verification as soon as possible.

(3) The annual operating expenses of the school are donated by the school board of directors, accounting for about 40% of the total annual income, which is not a long-term plan. It is urgent to raise funds to consolidate the foundation. The accounting records should be thoroughly reorganized.

(4) The equipment of the school's drawing and engineering department is simple and should be strengthened. A practical art factory should be actively prepared to be realized as soon as possible.

(5) The treatment of the school's teachers should be improved. It is commendable that teachers can implement make-up classes for leave on weekdays, but leave should not occur frequently.

(6) Too many students are absent from class. Strict measures should be taken to stop this. The management and training methods on weekdays must be comprehensive. The level of new students is too low. In the future, enrollment should be strictly recorded.

Private Zhongshan Physical Education College

Special reminders of the key points for improvement required by the school are as follows:

(1) Although the school's funds have slightly increased since the approval for establishment, efforts should still be made to raise more funds for development. Too little is allocated for expenses and teaching material; attempts should be made to supplement this according to the Ministry's set standards.

(2) The school's plan to rebuild all school buildings should be actively pursued to ensure its early realization. The existing school buildings, including the dining hall, kitchen, and toilets, are unhygienic and should be improved entirely.

(3) The school lacks teaching staff. More full-time instructors with superior academic knowledge and rich experience should be hired.

(4) The school has been overly lenient in admitting specialist students, resulting in a generally low level of student proficiency. There are very few students whose notes are detailed, well-organized, and clear. In the future, the school must strictly conduct entrance examinations. The students' coursework and the instructors' teaching should be rigorously assessed regularly. The number of specialist students admitted this year should not exceed thirty at most, as a means of restriction. Furthermore, academic credentials of new and old students and the annual grades of old students should be reported on time.

Ministry of Education Order to All Schools

Organizing Career Placement Agencies

(Nanjing, 8th) The Ministry of Education issued an order to all departments, stating: The Ministry recently received a proposal from the Executive Yuan regarding the petition from graduates of various universities in Peiping requesting relief from unemployment and suggesting a fundamental solution. One of the suggestions was to issue a circular to all universities and social organizations nationwide to encourage them to establish career placement agencies to assist university graduates in finding employment. The issue of youth unemployment is extremely complex and cannot be resolved solely by a department or ministry. However, the request in the original petition for each school to establish a career placement agency is indeed one of the relief measures. Each school should investigate and handle it accordingly. In addition to the Ministry consulting with the National Economic Council to establish a National Academic Work Advisory Center and reporting back, this order is also being circulated for compliance.

News from Various Schools

Tongde Medical College: Tongde Medical College has been actively working for half a year to prepare for the construction of new school buildings and the addition of various facilities. In addition to acquiring the former Health Experiment Institute near the city center as school buildings, it is also reported that several acres of private land have been purchased to build a lecture hall and dormitory in order to make it as perfect as possible. Because students in each department are already full this semester, the number of new students is only a few dozen. However, in recent days, those applying for admission to the school have been extremely enthusiastic, exceeding the quota by several times.

Private Huahai Vocational High School: The Private Huahai Vocational High School in this city, with reference to various past experiences of vocational guidance in Europe and the United States and the needs of domestic careers, has created a career guarantee system, opening an era of career protection. Principal Qiu Hanping believes that if vocational school graduates are still unemployed, it is tantamount to vocational schools becoming manufacturing sites for the unemployed, which weakens the faith of fathers and elder brothers in vocational schools and loses the purpose of vocational schools. Therefore, in addition to collecting career preparation funds each semester, the school also raises a career preparation fund to ensure the reliable career prospects of graduates three years later. This fund is separately managed by a custodial committee and properly deposited in the bank. In the future, the school plans to make good use of this fund to create various businesses to accommodate graduates to work and settle in.

Chizhi Affiliated High School: Chizhi College Affiliated High School, in view of the frequent disasters and rural bankruptcy in recent years, in order to reduce the burden on students, the school board decided to reduce the tuition fees for all senior high school and junior high school students by ten yuan per person from the autumn semester of this year. The tuition fee for senior high school is 28 yuan per person, and the tuition fee for junior high school is 20 yuan per person. The new student enrollment examination is scheduled to be held on the 17th of this month.

National Shanghai Medical College: National Shanghai Medical College, under the dedicated management of Dean Yan Fuqing, has achieved remarkable results. The faculty is particularly outstanding. Dr. Hu Mei, a newly hired special professor of internal medicine, has now arrived at the college. Dr. Hu has served as the president of Hunan Yale University, the president of Xiangya Medical College, the president of the New York Medical Institute, and the president of New York Hospital. He has profound academic knowledge and rich experience. This time, he has been hired to come to China to serve as a teaching researcher and consultant to the dean, assisting Dean Yan in planning everything. He will make a considerable contribution to the construction of the new college building on Observatory Road. Zhu Zuozhi, a newly hired associate professor of parasitology, holds a Bachelor of Science degree from Lingnan University, a Master of Science degree from Yenching University, a Ph.D. from Johns Hopkins University in the United States, and is a researcher in public health. He specializes in intestinal worm studies and has also arrived at the college. In addition, Dr. Tan Galili, a professor of anatomy at the University of Vienna in Austria, is an authority in the anatomy department and has been hired to lecture. He will arrive at the college soon. Zhang Jun, a newly hired associate professor of physiology, has studied at the University of Chicago in the United States for many years and is highly valued by Dr. Garin, the director of the physiology department. He will also arrive at the college soon. Dr. Wang Yihui, a newly hired professor of obstetrics and gynecology, has served as a professor at Peking Union Medical College for many years. His qualifications and reputation are well-known. He has now arrived at the college. Mrs. Wang Yihui, a newly hired associate professor of bacteriology, has also arrived at the college with her husband to take up her post.

Mingchen Elementary School, Xinqiaotou, Nanshi: Mingchen Elementary School is located in an industrial area, and 80 to 90 percent of the children are out of school. In order to popularize mass education, the school has set up a night school. The students are crowded and it is very developed. The principal wants to implement his original intention of serving the community, so he held the second variety show on the 5th of this month at 7:00 PM. There are many programs, and he pays more attention to the literacy movement, such as dramas about the suffering of illiteracy. Those who come to the school to get admission tickets are coming one after another.

Huiling Middle School: Huiling Middle School's junior high school department, since moving to the new address at 288 Maigen Road, has renovated the school buildings and started working. On July 31st, the first entrance examination for new male and female students was held. The number of people admitted will be announced soon. Because there are still vacancies in each grade, a second recruitment examination will be held on August 31st. Late applications will not be accepted. The affiliated elementary school department is also ready and has started enrollment. There are quite a few applicants. Furthermore, in view of the economic recession in recent years, in order to reduce the burden on the parents of each student, the tuition fee for senior high school students has been reduced from the original 40 yuan to 35 yuan, and the tuition fee for junior high school students has been reduced from the original 35 yuan to 25 yuan, so as to broaden the opportunities for education.

Handball Master Zheng Guiguang

Second Performance Today

Lost to Sun Daosheng Yesterday

Against Hong Yukui Today

Zheng Guiguang, a famous handball master from overseas Chinese in Honolulu, played his first performance match with Sun Daosheng, a veteran of the China YMCA, at the YMCA handball room at 4:00 PM yesterday. He will play his second performance match with Hong Yukui, a good player of the YMCA, at 5:00 PM today. Mr. Zheng is leaving Shanghai soon, and this may be one of his last battles.

The Process of the Battle: The long-quiet YMCA handball court suddenly attracted many spectators. After the two sides clashed, Zheng scored a few points first. Soon, Sun gradually advanced, and the situation became confrontational. After a score of ten to ten, Sun used his ingenious skills to rise sharply, arousing the infinite interest of the spectators. Sun won the first game 21 to 12. In the second game, Sun took advantage of his victory and took the lead. Zheng suddenly made a surprising move, sweeping away everything in his path and becoming invincible, and immediately reversed the score to 11 to 6. At this time, Sun's will was calm and his skills were agile. He used his strengths to overcome his opponent's weaknesses. After five or six rounds, Sun regained the advantage and won the final game. Sun also won 21 to 12. As a result, Sun won two to zero.

Overview of Ball Skills: Mr. Zheng is an all-around athlete from Honolulu, especially good at handball. His right hand kills have a thousand pounds of pressure. He can hit the north wall and counterattack as he pleases, and his rescues are as fast as lightning. He is truly worthy of his reputation. Mr. Sun is a veteran handball player of the YMCA. For more than ten years, he has used his left and right hands as if they were flying. He can see people's shortcomings and take advantage of them easily. His serves are ingenious and difficult to counterattack. Therefore, the competition between the two was extremely urgent. Sun's final victory was entirely due to his skillful use of his strengths.

Today's Program: At 5:00 PM this afternoon, Zheng Guiguang will play his second performance match with Hong Yukui, a good player of the YMCA. Hong is the most promising young man in the Shanghai handball world. He has many strengths and can compete with Mr. Zheng. Who will win is another highlight.

North China Swimming Competition

Beijing Athletes May Participate

(Beiping, 7th) The Sports Committee held an emergency meeting at 3:00 PM on the 7th to discuss the issue of Beijing athletes registering late for the 18th North China Swimming Competition. Le Yongnian, the director of the social affairs bureau's middle school, attended the meeting to explain the process. After discussion, it was believed that according to the Sports Committee's regulations, late registration had no room for compromise. However, (1) the registration deadline fell on a Sunday, and (2) the nature of the team and individual was slightly different. The competition location is in Beijing, and it would be contrary to the purpose of promoting sports if Beijing athletes were excluded. It was necessary to seek remedies. As a result, representatives from the five units of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Rehe, and Harbin suggested to the conference that they be allowed to participate in the conference. The conference has accepted, but according to the rules of the Sports Committee, it must be approved by a joint meeting before a decision can be made. The conference has scheduled a joint meeting on the 10th to discuss the matter.

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

A Word of Contribution

From Face to Legs and Feet

— Yang An

Where do imported cosmetics go? Even legs and feet are now made up!

Recently, a staff member of a major cosmetics company in Peiping (Beijing) reported: Currently, there are three types of leg makeup products used by women in Peiping. The first is nail polish for toenails, available in red, blue, purple, and yellow, all colors are complete, French products, each bottle costs two to seventeen or eighteen yuan. The second is skin fragrance cream, which is applied to the legs, ankles, insteps, heels, and toes, its purpose is to moisturize the skin, its fat content is especially rich compared to face creams, if applied properly, it is not difficult to become like solidified fat, the best of this cream costs five to twenty yuan per bottle. The third is flesh-colored powder, which is used after applying the cream, its purpose is to cool, dry, and brighten, therefore, once the makeup of the legs is completed, each time takes more than an hour, costing three to more than ten yuan, and the result is that it consumes a lot of foreign goods, and shakes the youth, therefore, although Peiping Mayor Yuan Liang banned women from going barefoot with bare legs, even though we merchants suffer a temporary loss, it is of great benefit to the social economy and national wealth. This news is very interesting, but very alarming, because such modern women like to be fashionable, resulting in several phenomena, directly:

(1) The import of cosmetics, creams, and perfumes in the first half of this year was 850,000 yuan.

(2) The import of perfumes and creams in June alone was 144,044 yuan.

(3) The lace for fashionable women's clothing in the first half of this year was 577,962 yuan.

(4) Several domestic sock factories are suffering from poor business and are asking the government to ban bizarre costumes.

(5) Men's burdens are increasing day by day, debts are increasing, and those who break promises, commit fraud, abscond, and commit suicide are also increasing in number. Indirectly:

(1) Rural bankruptcy is becoming more rapid.

(2) Domestic industries are increasingly overwhelmed by foreign goods.

(3) The national economy is increasingly shrinking, gradually entering a state of depletion.

(4) Foreigners leave fully loaded, manufacturing guns, cannons, and airplanes, in addition to economic aggression, and then military aggression.

Modern women, with a smile, can ruin finance and weaken national power to such an extent. The magic power of modern women is indeed considerable. Like mother, like daughter. Where there are modern women, there are modern children. The import of foreign toys in the first half of the year was also more than 570,000 yuan. This is all the blood and sweat of the people, brazenly rewarding foreigners without stinginess, what a heartbreaking thing. In this National Products Year, this phenomenon is even more distressing. In fact, it is best not to use rouge, powder, and face cream. If you do use them, there are domestic products, why must you use foreign goods as a glory. All these makeup products, used to apply to the face, already feel extravagant, but now they want to apply them to the legs and feet, to win the appreciation of men, what is their intention? It is perplexing to think about. I know that women's patriotism will not lag behind others, perhaps they do not know the gains and losses in this, it is up to family mothers and sisters, school teachers, social leaders, and groups enthusiastic about national products, based on the spirit of loving national products, using eloquent words, to persuade people they meet, without fear of tiring their lips, if everyone can be vigilant and change the atmosphere, perhaps next year's import report can save this improper expenditure, save bankrupt rural areas, and support the vitality of industry and commerce, so that in the Women's National Products Year, some achievements can be seen, I think that at this time, modern women will not be criticized by the world, and scolded by people.

Talking about National Products

Psychological Construction of the National Products Movement

— Nanguo Jiaren

In recent years, the number of small merchants selling odd pieces of cloth in the inland rural areas has been increasing day by day, but their profits have been decreasing day by day. According to the moans of those merchants, selling inferior goods is more profitable. If they wholesale national products purely, they cannot even sell enough to cover the cost. The reason is very simple: the honest and cowardly old people in the rural areas have not heard the tragic cries of their countrymen who have lost their country in the Northeast, they have not seen the ruined walls of Zhabei and Wusong, their concept of the enemy is still vague. They do not have the ability to distinguish between national products and foreign goods. In order to save a few copper coins to buy oil and rice, they would rather buy those cheap and beautiful foreign goods to make new clothes for their innocent children.

In terms of daily necessities, we all know that: some foreign goods are genuinely expensive compared to domestic products; some foreign goods are of the same quality as domestic products, but much cheaper. The reason why it's like this is due to other's lower production costs and the higher costs for domestic products. Merchants cannot ignore capital, and the poor consumers, for their own livelihood, are penny-pinching. So promoting national products has become just a nice-sounding slogan.

Since the national products movement aims solely to stimulate national consumption of domestic industrial products, the fundamental solution lies in reducing production costs so that the prices of national products are at least lower than those of the same products from foreign merchants or foreign factories in China. The methods to reduce production costs lie in improving production technology and adjusting tariffs. These two important tasks depend on the active struggle of the domestic industrial sector and the domestic government. This is not an easy task in the short term. Therefore, during this transition period, the consuming public should awaken a kind of national spirit to earnestly engage in the psychological construction of consuming national products.

The psychological analysis of people who like to use imported goods can be summarized as follows: among the people in the bourgeoisie, it is nothing more than (1) love of luxury; (2) love of fashion; (3) love of good goods that are durable. In the common people, in addition to having the above three psychologies, they also have (1) the psychology of being greedy for cheap things; (2) the psychology of liking good looks; (3) the psychology of not being responsible.

People who like to use imported goods are not ignorant people, perhaps they have a lot of superior intelligence. Their psychology may be that China will not be destroyed because one person likes to use foreign goods; nor will it suddenly become a rich and powerful country because one person uses all domestic products. Their psychology is that giving up cheap and beautiful imported goods to buy only domestic products is an invisible loss to personal or family finances, which is not something a smart person does.

These morbid psychologies are the great enemies of the national products movement. They are much stronger than the tangible power of enemy planes and cannons. We must correct them!

"Start with Myself"

— Xiao Bai

| A Message to Women Across the Country |

"The evolution of history is always forward." If we base ourselves on this sentence, stand at this stage, grasp reality, and go on a pilgrimage to "promote national products," then I think the display of facts will definitely make you feel extremely disappointed. Of course, here, let's not talk about anything else, just take the past seven months of this "Women's National Products Year," there has been no good news about the development of the national products, but the voices of foreign goods flooding and selling like crazy are constantly disturbing our ears. The International Trade Bureau recently announced that the import surplus for the first six months of this year was 30 million yuan, of which women's luxury goods such as perfumes, creams, and cosmetics accounted for more than 970,000 yuan, and the lace used for cheongsam trimming also reached 600,000 yuan, and the import of imported silk and satin is countless. The only result we hoped for from the women's community is such an alarming performance, which is enough to make us not only "disappointed" but also feel deeply "heartbroken."

However, why is the progress of national products so stagnant and difficult to develop? Then I dare say that the crux of the problem is purely obscured by a kind of bad psychology. The fact is that there are countless Chinese people who hold this kind of inferior mentality. They think that there are more than 450 million people in the country! My personal use of foreign goods to take advantage of some cheap things is irrelevant to the overall situation and will not affect the rise and fall of the entire economy. Therefore, they use foreign goods and enemy goods in a big way. But they don't know that assuming every Chinese person is like this, as long as each person's import surplus is two yuan per year, the total of 450 million people is already an astonishing 900 million yuan. Then think about it, should this bad idea of ours still exist? I'm afraid that the more it exists, the more our flesh and blood will be exploited by others, and the closer we will be to the day of national subjugation and family destruction.

Therefore, from this very good lesson, the psychology of "starting with myself" has also become the only way to remedy the reality. Originally, promoting national products is entirely based on practical work, everyone must be determined, everyone must work hard. This year is designated as "Women's National Products Year," and people's hopes for the women's community are very deep and earnest. Then I, as a housewife, should understand this point even more, fundamentally repent of my previous "selfish" thoughts, and based on the spirit of "starting with myself," vow to use national products from today onwards to reverse the misfortune of this "Women's National Products Year" and create a glorious page.

Community Education Personnel Should Take the Responsibility of Promoting National Products

— Ba Ling

Talking about the issue of national products, everyone said in unison: "Promoting national products naturally requires the joint efforts of people across the country, and those in power should lead by example, then the virtue of a gentleman, like the wind, will spread throughout the country, and its effect will be even greater, but the fundamental problem is that we still believe that we should start with education, and do our best to instill the concept of using national products in children's education, to lay a deep-rooted foundation for the future of national products, of course, is a great long-term plan, but in order to save the current crisis of the national products movement, social education should especially take on the responsibility of promoting and using national products.

New Hope for National Products

— Shi Ying

Page 16

Because the people who serve in community education agencies are in contact with the general public every day, what they hear and see has a greater impact…" This argument, the reporter believes, is worthy of discussion.

Everyone knows that the staff of community education agencies have the responsibility of training the masses, educating the masses, and guiding the masses, their mission is very important. Therefore, it is inevitable for community education staff to be in contact with the masses from time to time. When in contact with the masses, the first thing to do is to give the general public a good impression. If a community education worker in a suit and leather shoes runs to the countryside to talk to the masses, the timid masses will have already fled and dare not approach you, even if the masses who come to approach you, you can't arouse their belief and sympathy no matter what, not only that, I am afraid that you will also get bad ideas? There used to be a joke that a community education agency in a certain place once held a national products exhibition. When the meeting was held, quite a few people came. A gentleman in a Western suit went up to give a speech, advocating the importance of national products, before he could say anything, a member of the public in the crowd stood up and questioned: "Today is a national products movement, we do not welcome rich old men in Western suits to come on stage to speak," this caused the sympathy of the whole audience, and this friend in a Western suit, turned red in the face, retreated in embarrassment, this is a real situation, it can be a serious lesson for community education personnel, from this matter, it can be seen how important it is to lead by example? The compass of national community education personnel, especially the leaders of a community education agency, everyone should be like this, everyone should be like this, then, approaching the general public, what they say is especially effective, at the same time, wearing national products clothing and talking to the public about promoting national products is especially pleasant to hear, especially to make people believe, this is something that national community education personnel must pay attention to.

Finally, I sincerely hope that the leaders of national community education agencies and comrades who are dedicated to social education will all take on the responsibility of promoting and using national products, then, the virtue of a gentleman, like the wind, can naturally influence the general public.

Thinking of Huishan Clay Figures from the Import of Toys

— Zhang Mengzhao

In the National Products Year, amidst the calls for promoting national products, foreign goods are coming in an endless stream, this is really a strange phenomenon in our country! It is also a unique shame that our country cannot wash away! Great humiliation!

According to a report released by the International Trade Bureau on August 2, the import of games and toys in the first six months of this year was 292.195 gold units, equivalent to 577,962 yuan in national currency, which is a significant increase compared to the import of 233.188 gold units in the first six months of last year.

If children's toys must be bought from foreign countries, it is enough to cultivate in children the psychology of buying foreign goods and despising domestic goods. Who should be responsible for this?

From the import of toys, I think of our Wuxi Huishan clay figures. The development of handicrafts, those who travel to Wuxi all know that the small clay toys are all ingenious and lifelike, what birds, beasts, ancient sages! All kinds of Peking Opera, exquisitely crafted, but unfortunately they cannot be scientificized, using models for casting, without research by soil scientists! There is no large-scale organized toy company, no other agencies that promote them effectively, and finally, they are stuck in their ways! There is no ability to export them abroad! Seeing foreign toys anesthetizing our children! It is really a heartbreaking thing! I hope to start with improving Huishan clay figures and promoting Huishan clay figures, collecting self-made toys from all over the country, and we will launch a movement to clear out foreign toys! By this time next year, we will no longer see the alarming numbers of toy imports!

Talking about Women's National Products Year from the Consumption of Lace

— Yao Chengxuan

Zhuangzi said: "There is no greater sorrow than the death of the heart." Time is passing like water, and there are only four months left from beginning to end! I hope that women will have some achievements in this short period and become a model.

Promoting National Products Should Show More National Products Films

— Yu Youqing

When we promote national products, we should not only pay attention to clothing, food, and goods, but we should pay attention everywhere, and even in terms of entertainment, we should also care about national products. For example, when hosting banquets and socializing, we do not necessarily have to use foreign alcoholic beverages, the things produced in our China are not necessarily inferior to imported goods! Secondly, the import of cosmetics is also extremely alarming, why bother to give useful money to others for the cost of guns and bombs? In order to save the rights and interests of the motherland from overflowing, everyone should pay attention to national products and not like to buy other people's things, thinking it is luxurious.

I am a movie fan, I like to watch movies. Fortunately, my appetite is the same, regardless of good or bad, regardless of superiority or inferiority, as long as I have the time, I will go to the movie theater. Fortunately, the movies in Suzhou are cheap and beautiful, so every Saturday and Sunday, I have become a regular customer of the movie theater. Sometimes I am invited by friends, and I also go to enjoy them in the remaining days. Perhaps Chinese people's psychology of worshiping foreign films is more intense! Even people who do not understand English (this refers to talkies) also like to watch foreign films, listening to difficult to understand languages seems to surpass national films, I do not know what this psychology is?

I happened to flip through the local supplement of a certain newspaper on July 30, in which the movie theaters showing foreign films accounted for three-quarters, which shows the worship of foreign films by the people of Shanghai. But even in the interior, Suzhou is not the same? It seems that after watching a foreign film, even if the plot is sometimes incomprehensible, many people think it is very interesting! The expenditure of this money, when I think about it, is no less than the import of cosmetics! But to clarify my intention, we are not rejecting foreign films, at least we should show more domestic films, so that Chinese films can progress and flourish, otherwise, foreign films will fill the market, and Chinese films will not be hit? In all conscience, some companies in China produce films that are not so bad, and are worth watching at least to some extent. Since there are domestic films to watch, then why spend tens of thousands of money to give to others? Therefore, my argument is that to promote national products, we should show national products films, which is also a very valuable issue, and has a lot to do with the Chinese economy. People who care about the future of national products should think about how to reverse the psychology of the Chinese people to value national films.

Finally, I am not criticizing the badness of foreign films, I think nine out of ten foreign films are sensual films of the kind with flying jade legs and prominent breasts, which makes young people a little demonic to see, this is the truth, I like to say it thoroughly, except for military films, most are sensual films, under the guidance of the new life in China, I think people in the new life should work hard and strive to be strong, and advance aggressively, is it possible to lose their souls under the flying jade legs and prominent breasts? (Of course, I am even more opposed to dance troupes)

From this point of view, people who are enthusiastic about national products should also pay attention to promoting national products, and should show more national products films, this issue is somewhat worthy of discussion?

Short story

Yellow Mud Ridge

— Rong Yu

Daytime: Singing Songs of Grievance, a Resourceful Star Delivering Patriotic Speeches

The scorching sun burns like fire, half the rice in the fields withers. The farmers’ hearts are like boiling water: Young masters and noble sons wave their fans.

It is said that Bai Rishu, Bai Sheng, carrying a wine peddler’s pole, sang that folk song as he walked along the Yellow Mud Ridge road. It was midday, the sun blazing fiercely, with not a cloud in the sky. He was so tired that beads of sweat as big as soybeans hung from his temples. However, the sight of one hundred thousand strings of gold and jewels glittered before him, making him forget the heat. Ignoring whether it was against the law, he felt light on his feet and full of energy, walking step by step up the ridge. When he reached the pine forest, there was no sign of Yang Zhi's group, only Chao Gai, Wu Yong, Gongsun Sheng, Liu Tang, and the three Ruan brothers, seven men in total, disguised as date merchants. They had several Jiangzhou carts and were also waiting. Bai Sheng greeted the seven men, panting, and said, "Could it be that those guys didn't take this road? Otherwise, they should have arrived." Chi Fa Gui Liu Tang said, "I heard reliably that they would definitely come this way. Perhaps there were some mishaps along the way, so they were delayed." Ruan Xiaoqi shouted loudly, "To hell with it! We'll wait here, even for ten days or half a month. If other merchants pass by, we'll give them a small profit first, and we'll at least get some grease." Chao Gai nodded in agreement. As they were talking, Ruan Xiaoer pointed to the hillside to the north and said, "Isn't that a group of people coming? It might be Yang Zhi sending the treasure to us." Wu Yong instructed them to keep their voices down and follow the plan. After a short while, the group reached the bottom of the pine forest. The heat was unbearable, so they unloaded their burdens and sat down in the shade. Ruan Xiaowu, wielding a broadsword, jumped out of the forest and shouted at the group, "Those who know what's good for them, leave your toll money!" When the group saw Ruan Xiaowu's ferocious appearance and aggressive manner, one of them crawled to the ground begging for mercy. Several of the bolder ones pleaded, "Great King! Have pity on us, we used up our capital and energy to go to Hebei to sell local products, planning to go to Tokyo to earn some money. Who knew that there would be heavy customs duties and extortion along the way? The cost of these goods is already not light. Whether we can sell them in Tokyo is still a question. Nowadays, the noble sons and daughters don't like our local products, instead, they are making goods for those red-haired merchants. We have already suffered enough, where would we get gold and silver to offer to you Great Kings!" Ruan Xiaowu glared and said, "I don't care about that. Give money if you have it, give your life if you don't." As he spoke, he thrust his broadsword down. At that moment, Wu Xuejiu from the forest, who had been listening for a long time, jumped out and said, "Brothers, don't be rash, listen to me. These merchants are selling local products, whether they make money or lose money, the money is always in their own pockets. Like a Chu bow being found by a Chu person, it doesn't harm the country's lifeline. Moreover, they are not greedy for heavy profits and are unwilling to give money to foreigners, truly commendable and praiseworthy for their patriotism. Although we robbers have no conscience, we also have hearts. How can we lay a cruel hand on such admirable people? It's just a pity that the current officials are muddleheaded, only knowing to exploit these people, not protecting them, instead, letting those red-haired merchants act rampant, using worthless goods to cheat our money, using our money to recruit soldiers and buy horses, and store up grain. In three to five years, they will definitely start a war. Do you think this is painful or not!" As Wu Yong said this, Ruan Xiaoqi jumped out from the side and shouted loudly, "Isn't this infuriating! We don't want to rob any birthday gifts or be greedy for wealth, let's go up the mountain to kill those red-haired foreigners!" Wu Yong waved his hand again and said, "Brothers, don't be impatient. These red-haired foreigners are just doing business, they haven't committed any major crimes, we have no reason to kill them. We should lead by example, not using red-haired goods ourselves. Then we should punish those profiteering merchants who sell smuggled goods, and those who love using foreign goods, that's the right thing to do!" Everyone nodded in agreement upon hearing these words. If you want to know what happens next? There's no explanation in the next installment, readers can guess for themselves!

National Goods Drama

Soda

— Han Yu

Characters: Customer, Shop Assistant

Time: Afternoon of a certain day in the summer of the 23rd year

Setting: A refreshment shop, with a shop assistant tending the store. (The curtain opens, a customer enters from outside.)

Customer: Get me a bottle of soda!

Shop Assistant: What brand do you want?

Customer: (Sitting down) Of course, XXX. What good are Chinese goods?

Shop Assistant: Chinese goods aren't bad either. The fizz is strong enough!

Customer: (Showing impatience) I only want XXX. (Pointing inside) Hurry up and get it.

Shop Assistant: (Enters without a word), (Takes out a soda, pours it into a glass, places it in front of the customer) Sir! Isn't this flavor good?

Customer: (Drinking and speaking) XXX is definitely better than Chinese goods! Look at how good foreign goods are.

Shop Assistant: (Smiling) Sir! Please forgive me, because I did something deceptive. Do you think this is XXX? It's not, it's a domestic product!

Customer: (Appearing surprised) This is really a domestic product? How is the taste almost the same as foreign goods?

Shop Assistant: Sir! It's all in the psychology. If you think domestic goods are good, then when you drink domestic goods, you will feel they are good. If you think domestic goods are bad, then when you drink domestic goods, you will also feel they are bad. You often think foreign goods are good, then unconsciously when you drink them, you will also think they are foreign goods. In reality, domestic goods and foreign goods are not much different.

Customer: (Slightly ashamed), Quick! Bring another bottle! (Curtain closes)

Introduction to National Products

Introducing a type of summer shoes

— Bian Beichen

Shoes, especially women's shoes, because they want to make themselves more beautiful, they do not hesitate to sacrifice a lot of money to buy foreign leather shoes. Although there are also many made by Chinese people, the raw materials are inevitably imported!

If we make a detailed statistics of the raw materials imported over the years, it will be a very shocking number.

Now it is summer, and the general modern ladies and misses are wearing the most popular European and American leather shoes that expose their toes. It is said that the only reason is that they are cool, comfortable, and beautiful, but in the coolness, comfort, and beauty, they unconsciously send many airplanes and cannons to foreigners.

Let me introduce a kind of purely domestic shoes, the raw materials are made of flower ribbons and white cloth soles; they can also expose the toes and are cool, comfortable and beautiful. In the past, they were adopted by monks and nuns, but recently most of the women in this city wear them, and their beauty is not inferior to imported leather shoes.

It is said that the purchase of the shoes is in the larger temples and stores selling Buddhist supplies everywhere.

Now I will write the advantages of the shoes below: (1) The price is fair, only four or five corners of silver per pair.

(2) The material is light and easy to travel long distances;

(3) Completely domestic products, no leaks.

Finally, I sincerely hope that general movie stars, dance queens, social butterflies, will unanimously promote them; at the same time, I hope that women! come to purchase them unanimously.

National Goods News

National goods vending places along the Longhai Railway

— Wang Shouqiu

The Longhai Railway Administration recently held national product vending places along the Longhai Railway to promote national products, and now a charter has been drafted to invite merchants to undertake it. This initiative is really good news for women's national goods year, and other roads can follow suit. The following is a selection of the charter for reference by followers.

Article 1: In order to promote national products and develop the national economy, this road has designated suitable locations inside each station to invite merchants to rent and establish national product vending places to sell local products and handicrafts from various stations, so that passengers can choose and buy at any time. Article 2: Merchants from all over the country who wish to undertake this vending place should first apply to the road traffic department for a license, and sign a lease contract in accordance with the road's land leasing regulations before they can start business. When applying for the above-mentioned license, a deposit shall be paid in accordance with Article 2. Article 3: The area occupied by each station vending place shall not exceed six square meters. The rent and deposit are stipulated as follows: (A) First-class stations: Lianyungang, Sunjiashan, Dapu, Xuzhou, Kaifeng, Zhengzhou, Luoyang East Station, Shanzhou, Tongguan, a total of ten stations. Monthly rent is five corners per square meter, and the deposit is one hundred yuan. (B) Second-class stations: Xinpu, Haizhou, Canal, Commercial Port, Zhongmu, Xunshui, Gong County, Luoyang West Station, Huixing Town, Lingbao, a total of ten stations, monthly rent is three corners per square meter, and the deposit is sixty yuan. (C) Third-class stations: Except for the above-mentioned regulations in Group A and B, the remaining stations are listed in Group C, with a monthly rent of two corners per square meter and a deposit of forty yuan. Article 4: The location of the vending place shall be designated by the road traffic department. Article 5: If the vending place's location interferes with the road's affairs, regardless of whether the vending place has been established or not, it may be designated to move to another suitable location within a certain period of time. If the contractor refuses to comply, the license may be revoked and the rent paid may be confiscated. Article 6: The contractor shall build a mobile wooden house in the designated location to operate the vending place. The wooden house shall be planned by the government, and the contractor shall build it according to the plan, and shall not be simple and lose its beauty. Article 7: The vending place is dedicated to promoting local products and handicrafts and selling national products. It shall not sell imported goods. If imported goods are found, the road may seal them up and order them to be removed. Article 8: If the vending place secretly operates improper businesses or sells prohibited items, the road may immediately stop all its rights upon detection. The deposit paid, as well as the rent for the incomplete month, shall be used as a fine and will not be refunded. In serious cases, it shall be transferred to the local government for handling in accordance with the law. Article 9: The various items listed in the vending place shall be opened in accordance with the local market price and a detailed and uniform price list shall be reviewed and approved by the road traffic department and hung on the wall. It is not allowed to arbitrarily increase prices and deceive customers. Article 10: The vending place's business personnel shall wear specially made clothing and badges to make it easy for passengers to recognize, and a list of names shall be opened, with two three-inch photos attached to each person, and sent to the road traffic department for verification and issuance of a license to enter and exit the platform. The style of clothing badges shall be determined by the road to ensure uniformity. Article 11: The vending place's business and related cleaning, hygiene, and fire protection matters shall be subject to the supervision and command of the road health inspector and the station chief road police. Article 12: If the vending place contractor violates any of the articles in this charter, the road may stop all its rights at any time.
