Free Talk

Random Notes on Reading (II)

— Yan Yu

Even in the same era and the same country, people can say things that others cannot understand.

Barbusse has a very interesting short story called "Native Language and Foreign Language," which records how a wealthy family in France entertained three soldiers who had gone through life and death in the European War. The lady of the house came out to greet them, but they had nothing to say. They forced themselves to say a few words, but they had nothing to answer. They only felt that they were sitting in a large room and were careful enough to hurt their bones. It was not until they sneaked back to their own "pigsty" that they felt comfortable all over, talking and laughing, and in the German prisoners, they discovered people who spoke their "our language" through gestures.

Because of this experience, one soldier vaguely thought: "There are two worlds in this world. One is the world of war. The other is the world of clean kitchens, beautiful houses, like chapels with safe-deposit boxes. It is a completely different world. A different country. Inside, there live strange-thinking foreigners."

What the lady later said to a gentleman was: "It is impossible to talk to them. It seems that there is an insurmountable abyss between them and us."

In fact, it is not necessary for the lady and the soldiers to be like this. Even we—whether considered "feudal remnants" or "compradors" or anything else—and almost the same kind of people, as long as there are some differences in some places, and if we have to be of one mind, we often cannot help but have nothing to say to each other. However, we Chinese are smart, and some people have already invented a panacea, which is "The weather today... hahaha!" If it is a banquet, we only guess fists and do not make any arguments.

From this point of view, it may be really difficult for literature to be universal and permanent. "The weather today... hahaha!" Although it is somewhat universal, it is very doubtful whether it can be permanent, and it does not look much like literature. So a superb writer has set a rule for himself, pushing all those who do not understand his "literature" out of "humanity" in order to maintain its universality. Literature also has other characteristics, but he is unwilling to say it, so he has no choice but to use this method. However, in this way, "literature" exists, but there are not many "people".

So it is said that the more superb the literature, the fewer people who understand it. At the extreme of superbness, universality and permanence only converge on the author alone. However, the writer becomes sad again, saying that he is spitting blood. There is really no way to imagine it.

Night Notes from the Borderlands (Part 1)

— Wu Yan

They should have spent the night in the town of "Yache Xun," but fearing an attack by mountain bandits, the merchant escort team advanced another ten miles in the dim twilight of the small wilderness. By the time the men and horses approached Qingkou, the deep blue night sky was already full of blossoming, radiant star flowers.

Qingkou is a small village facing the main road, and the residents are all farmers. When the merchant escort team's storm lanterns swayed with long white light, slowly entering the village, short houses, round haystacks, and dark, dense miscellaneous trees appeared everywhere.

The village dog had just barked loudly, rushing over fiercely, but immediately let out a long howl and fled behind the house lurking in the night shadow. Then there were sudden sounds of doors closing everywhere, and the crying of children.

The village, quietly crouching under the starry sky, was awakened in an instant, trembling. The sweat of men and horses completely washed away the scent of flowers, plants, and resins that had previously been floating in the air.

Almost every household had brothers from the merchant escort team walking in, placing their guns in the corner of the room, and sitting or lying down on benches and tables at will. I was not very happy to rest with them, so I planned to find a remote little house—a place where the brothers from the merchant escort team did not like to go. As a result, I found it at the end of the village. The door was closed, and there was only a faint light in the house, leaking out from the cracks in the wooden walls. Perhaps she heard my footsteps, the light in the house suddenly went out, but I did not care whether the owner of the house welcomed me or not, and went straight forward to knock on the door. After a while, because the door was knocked too hard, I heard an old woman's voice, trembling, saying, "Have pity on us! There is nothing left here!... Alas, great merciful Bodhisattva!"

"Old Mama, don't be afraid, I'm here to borrow a place to stay,... I'm a good person!

After a period of silence, perhaps she was beginning to examine me through the crack in the door, she made a breathless sound, but slightly calmer than just now.

"Then, then, guest, please go to another house,... it's terribly narrow here!"

"Old Mama, other houses are full of people, please let me stay for one night, I'll give you money."

Seeing that she was still doubting me, I pleaded very sincerely. She did not answer, I only felt the sound of her footsteps lightly響to 裏面went. I stood for a while, planning to leave, but suddenly heard someone coming out from 裏面, a man's voice saying this.

"Old Mama, it doesn't matter, everything is looked after by the Bodhisattva, the Bodhisattva will take care of you!"

Impressions of Zibo

— Luo Wang

(6) The Life of Miners

In Zichuan, we saw countless people who looked like black slaves, or like "bumpkins" in a circus, their faces covered in black dirt, only revealing two big white eyes, looking at people! These people are coal miners!

We made some small visits to the life of miners, but did not get much information. But just to say about the miners of the Luda Company, there are many types, from going down the well to dig coal, underground transportation, screening workers, etc. Naturally, the workers who go down the well suffer the most. They go deep into the underground layer, 300 to 700 meters below. Their only good friend is a mine lamp! They work every day, day and night shifts are more than twelve hours, and the wages used to be good, about two or three yuan, but now they are only five or six mao to eight or nine mao per day!

What miners fear most is heavy rain, because this can cause water to flood the mine, with the fear of being drowned. Therefore, workers usually avoid the word "full." When pouring wine, "full" is only said to be "empty"! This is a special explanation in the life of miners!

There are even more miners in Boshan! Most residents rely on working as miners for a living! There are also countless coal loaders.

In the past, workers' lives were very prosperous because coal could be sold at a good price, and labor prices were therefore high. The old-style small-scale (most of which are still like this) mines would dig a tunnel about three feet high in winter, and the workers had to bend over and crawl on the ground to move forward. Although the work was hard, the reward was very rich. Workers often worked for one day, got two or three yuan in reward, and then rested for two days. Because money came easily, workers have always been living for the day, until the money was used up before going to grab the coal mine! At that time, the workers wore silk and ate oil, so there were many silk shops and restaurants in Boshan. When the great tide of the world's economic panic pressed tightly on the mining area, the dumping of foreign coal blocked the sales of Chinese coal, so labor prices gradually declined! In the past, just pushing coal dregs could earn more than two yuan a day, but now pushing it for a day is less than one yuan, the cost of living is gradually increasing, and income is gradually decreasing; so in Boshan, although there are big landlords who have made hundreds of thousands of fortunes by opening mines, at the same time, countless workers suffering from economic oppression have naturally been produced! So in Boshan, there are always people hanging themselves every day!

The place where we performed dramas was called Shanghetan, which is a kiln goods market! On weekdays (when there are no market days), it is said that no one easily passes by there, because every night you can hear ghosts crying and gods wailing. These words are of course rumors from the locals, but they can confirm that there are indeed many people who "hang themselves in the southeast branches"! Our partner once went to a forest and saw a person hanging high in the sky with his neck tied to the tree branch! This kind of death is caused by the social and economic situation. I don't want to make any arguments here, I just want to ask everyone to pay attention to the current facts!

Summer in Pubin Park

— Yi An writes

I Come From the East (18)

— Xingye

After the ship left Kobe, several Cantonese on the ship seriously considered the issue of landing. They had earned money in the United States for decades and were now returning to their hometown to retire. They were talking furtively in the smoking room, saying how terrible Shanghai was at night. If you have a gold ring on your finger, someone will pull you away. If you wear better clothes, someone will pour acid on you. If people know you have money, you will be kidnapped or killed. They told each other in whispers, as if a great disaster was imminent.

A Cantonese couple who had run a restaurant in Chicago were especially afraid. The wife was a young and somewhat romantic Chinese-American girl from San Francisco, and insisted on going to Shanghai that day. The husband was old and had earned tens of thousands of dollars. He felt that everywhere in China, hands were reaching out for his money or his life, so he insisted on spending the night on the ship and would not disembark until he reached Hong Kong. He told me that China was not good. When he opened a restaurant in Chicago, whenever someone came from China, they either wanted to raise money for schools or for airplanes. He had to spend thousands of dollars every year to deal with these things. I think what he said was sincere.

The setting sun shone on the yellow waves. A large group of passengers gathered on the deck, everyone harboring curiosity and fear about Shanghai. Two extremely thin shadows of the shore lined the mouth of the Yangtze River, the shore shadows closing on us, and gradually we saw three or five sailboats ahead. Approaching Wusongkou, everyone on deck pointed and talked about the situation during the Battle of Shanghai. The sailors on the ship, because they had witnessed the battle firsthand on the ship during the war, described it even more vividly. Everyone talked about this event like Investiture of the Gods or Romance of the Three Kingdoms. Curious Americans regretted not seeing this good show with their own eyes.

By the time we arrived at the Pudong Old Taikoo Wharf, it was already dusk. Coal smoke mixed with the evening mist, shrouding the entire city of Shanghai in a gray curtain. The Sassoon Mansion and the HSBC Bank, the Customs Clock Tower and the unfinished International Hotel, all revealed faint shadows. The Huangpu River was really narrow. When our postal ship turned around, the ship's body crossed the river, locking the entire river, making it difficult for any ships to come and go. I then thought of the story of the sunken ship in Lushun Port during the Russo-Japanese War. I also fantasized about various thought-provoking phenomena and strategies that would occur if an international war broke out in the Far East.

Shanghai is full of buzzing sounds. Of all the noisy ports in the world, this one is probably the first. In the evening, I hastily took a small motorboat from the Old Taikoo Wharf to the New Customs Wharf with a few friends from the ship. The small boat was crowded with people. The small river was crowded with boats. The roads were crowded with cars. It seemed that there was no room to move anywhere. The New Customs Wharf was even more crowded. It is a country with a small land area and a large population, but at the wharves of Kobe and Yokohama, you can barely see a few people. Commerce in New York and London must be more prosperous than Shanghai, but you will never be squeezed in a crowd when you arrive in New York and London. A population of 400 million is a formidable force, but if 400 million people are squeezed together in chaos, there is nothing to fear.

Regarding the "?" in the First Section of "Zibo Impressions"

Letter from Luo Wangjun:

The first section of this article mentions that the audience watching the play consisted of two to three "thousand" people! The editor added a "?" under the word "thousand," perhaps doubting the accuracy! However, it is common for our outdoor performances to attract two to three thousand people. This is an "actual number" and has a different meaning from the common phrase "tens of thousands of attendees" at general XX sports meets. Therefore, if anyone does not believe it, I can report further that when we screen movies in various counties, residents from twenty miles outside the city also come to watch, with at least ten thousand people every night, and sometimes up to thirty or forty thousand. A vast open space is filled with people sitting on the ground, all looking up at the silver screen. This is something that friends in the South might find hard to imagine, but in the hot, less-educated North, this kind of fact is not surprising!

Commercial News

Financial Circles Absorb Vast Amounts,

Cotton Yarn Soars to New Heights

Distant Months Discover a New Peak of 192 Yuan

The yarn market continues to rise, and the situation is becoming increasingly tight. This has been brewing for a long time, and once it erupts, it is difficult to contain. The biggest reason for this surge is partly due to the continuous procurement of current yarn from North and Central China. Dealers from Tianjin consider Chinese yarn to be cheaper than Japanese yarn and are particularly eager to acquire coarse yarn. Another factor is that all factories have reported being sold out of 16-count yarn, with some factories already experiencing shortages. Furthermore, the prices of flour and wheat have recently soared, leading to large profits for financial circles. As a result, they have changed their plans and are also absorbing large amounts in the cotton yarn market for speculation. Consequently, confidence is boosted, and buying surges, leading to the discovery of a new peak of 192 yuan for distant months.

Gold Rooster Jumps Wildly by Two or Three Yuan

The cotton yarn market opened with an unstoppable momentum. Buyers are showing great appetite, as financiers, having profited handsomely from flour and wheat, are now flocking to the cotton yarn market to buy in bulk. Simultaneously, spot yarn sales to customers are thriving daily, depleting factory inventories considerably. This boosts confidence, tightens the market, and causes short sellers to panic. The market already had the potential to rise earlier, but it was suppressed by Japanese merchants selling off and by the pressure of goods in cotton yarn warehouses, leading to a temporary slump. Recently, support from actual sales in the North has triggered new buying activity, and money houses are buying at market prices without price limits. The market suddenly surges wildly, rising higher and higher, with the upward trend intensifying. As a result, prices for all months rose by 2.478 jiao to 3.2 jiao. The total volume traded was 88,550 bales. Sales were as follows: Da Ji 2,550 bales, Xin Chang 1,500 bales, Yuan Da 1,250 bales, Jin Chang 2,250 bales, Ming De 1,350 bales, Chang Ji 1,750 bales, Jun Chang 1,250 bales, Sen Kang 1,550 bales, Tong Feng 1,150 bales, Heng De 950 bales, Ren Feng 2,750 bales, Yi Chang 5,800 bales, Heng Chang 4,650 bales, Xie Sheng 950 bales. The cotton market is trending upward, with the situation continuing to strengthen. Grains

Flour and Wheat Advance and Retreat Sharply

Yesterday, the flour market, after demanding margin calls the day before and closing for a day, saw the market sentiment become good due to the worsening environment and positive external news. Before the opening, it was anticipated that prices would surely rise. When trading opened in the morning, prices had already risen by around 1.12 yuan due to the continued increases in Canadian and Chicago quotes over the past two days. Therefore, the current month's opening price was raised sharply to 0.66 yuan. Distant months also trended upward, but to a lesser extent, around 0.35 yuan. Unexpectedly, after the second session, buying interest from outside the trade remained strong, and buyers absorbed supplies at any cost. By the third session, prices for all months, near and distant, had risen sharply again by 0.1 to 0.123 yuan compared to Monday's market. Prices for November and beyond were all above the 0.9 jiao level, demonstrating the extent of speculative frenzy. When trading opened in the afternoon, sentiment remained high, and the current month rose to 0.885 yuan. This was a record unseen in three or four years. Opening prices for September and October also continued to be strong by 0.12 yuan. However, it was rumored that factories were collectively selling off to maintain prices. At the highest point, they indeed sold off aggressively. As a result, while opening prices for November were good, prices fell sharply step by step. The situations for December and January were similar. The market was overbought, and sensing a change in wind direction, sellers dumped their holdings at the second session's opening. The sharpness of the reversal was as grand as the upward surge. From then on, prices fell in all sessions, especially for November and beyond, with the decline being even sharper. The difference from the morning reached 0.15 yuan. As a result, the current month was still better by 0.03 yuan compared to before the suspension, September and October were better by 0.0025 yuan, November fell by 0.0325 yuan, December fell by 0.035 yuan, and January fell by 0.01 yuan. The exchange has increased margin requirements again, effective yesterday, to 750 yuan for both buyers and sellers.

Yesterday in the wheat futures market, after opening in the morning, prices rose by around 1.12 yuan in Canadian and foreign wheat quotations over the past two days, leading to extremely strong sentiment. The opening price for the current month was 0.3 yuan, and September's was 0.4 yuan, an increase of around 0.17-0.18 yuan compared to before the suspension. However, in the current market, which has already entered a frenzy, this increase was not considered severe. However, after the second session, due to the continued wild increase in flour futures, the strength of buying interest was unparalleled. The current month rose to 0.42 yuan, September to 0.61 yuan, October to 0.73 yuan, and November/December to 0.73-0.74 yuan, an increase of 0.23-0.34 yuan compared to Monday's market. This kind of consecutive sharp rise was a first since the exchange was established. When trading opened in the afternoon, the current month continued to rise by 0.06-0.07 yuan initially. However, when the September opening price showed signs of weakness in flour futures, the opening prices for all months also fell. The current month fell to 0.3 yuan, and September fell to 0.44 yuan, with an average decline of 0.1-0.2234 yuan. However, prices were still higher compared to before the suspension. As a result, the current month rose by 0.2 yuan, September rose by 0.15 yuan, October rose by 0.08 yuan, November rose by 0.07 yuan, December rose by 0.06 yuan, and January rose by 0.16 yuan in the morning but fell back by the same amount in the afternoon. In the spot wheat market, with standard prices being high, sentiment was also good. High-quality wheat, such as that from Xuzhou, Shandong, was quoted at 4.4 yuan, while medium-quality wheat was quoted at around 2.3 yuan. A total of over 10,000 bags were opened. For inland packaged wheat, such as that from Suzhou, the asking price was already 7 yuan.

Jiujiang Dealers Vigorously Purchase Foreign Rice

North China Dealers Inquire About Jing Rice

The situation in the foreign rice market was initially strong, but due to sporadic arrivals in recent days, and with sudden rain in the city yesterday, sentiment turned downward, and market prices immediately fell. Slightly inferior Xiaojiao rice fell to 10.45 yuan. However, after the market price fell slightly, local buyers became greedy again, and with strong demand from inland areas, dealers from Jiangxi province became even more active. As soon as the market price fell, all parties competed to buy, and high-quality Xiaojiao rice rose sharply to 10.72 yuan, almost 1 jiao higher than the previous day. Other rice varieties showed little difference from previous market prices. However, new Hunan rough Jing rice opened at 8.4 yuan, Hankou rough rice opened at 8.5 yuan, while machine-milled Jing rice showed a slight decline, with prices opening at 11 yuan, and lower-quality varieties at 10.23 yuan. The total opening was 6,000 bags of Xiaojiao rice, 200 bags of Saigon rice, 1,500 bags of various rough rice, and 1,300 bags of machine-milled Jing rice. The primary destination was the Jiujiang area. In addition to continued procurement by local inland dealers, there were also 246 bags of newly packaged Jing rice inquired about by northern dealers, with a price of 10 yuan.

River Barges Carrying Rice are Delayed by Wind

Very Few Arrivals: Trade Also Quiet

(South Shanghai) Due to wind and tides obstructing sources from various areas, only four or five barges arrived yesterday, carrying about six to seven hundred shi of goods. The local market was also at a standstill because of this, with only a few dealers absorbing supplies. A Qingdao dealer suddenly selected 700-800 bags of special goods such as Qing Si. Market conditions were unremarkable. New Geng rice still opened at 11.2 yuan.

(North Shanghai) Eight or nine barges arrived yesterday from various locations downriver. Sales of all goods were obstructed by wind and rain, and little trading took place. White Geng rice was slightly lower by 0.1-0.2 yuan, while the remaining goods were flat. However, Dongxin Geng rice remained firm.

Soybean Price Increase Slows

Raw Soybean Oil Continues to Rise

Yesterday, the trend of rising soybean prices slowed down, mainly because of a decrease in downstream demand. A total of eleven or twelve cartloads of various soybeans were traded in the market, with sales mainly to small-scale local dealers. Factories were inactive, and prices rose by 0.15 yuan. Although telegrams reported higher prices in the afternoon, the market atmosphere remained subdued, leading to slightly hesitant sentiment. Only 160 bags of June white soybeans were traded, with prices rising by 0.3 yuan. Due to the intermittent supply of new soybeans from Jiujiang, holders of stored soybeans were waiting for higher prices. Therefore, there were no transactions, except for 60 bags re-sold by traders. City gate soybean prices opened at 4.4 yuan. The oil market differed from the soybean market due to rising production costs, interrupted supply, and relatively thin inventories. Therefore, market prices continued to rise. Soybean oil rose by 0.8 yuan, and peanut oil rose by 0.5 yuan. The future outlook is still strong.

Financial - Silver Price Increase Remains Strong

Gold Price Falls Again by 4.1 Yuan

The gold market has been trending downwards for several days. Yesterday, the silver price rose again, leading to a sharp decline in the gold market at the opening. However, buying interest was stronger after the decline, weakening the downward momentum and leading to a slight rebound. However, the situation remained uncertain throughout the morning, with supply and demand fluctuating, making it difficult to feel optimistic. At the opening, overseas silver markets in the UK and the US both rose, and the forward silver price on the Five Metals Exchange rose by 0.06-0.072. London spot gold fell by 2.5 pence, and exchange rates all increased. American cotton rose by 10 pounds, and American wheat rose by 1.25. Stock prices fell slightly. According to reports, the domestic disaster situation was severe after President Roosevelt's inspection, and the government would sacrifice 500,000 yuan to provide relief. Given this situation, the US government would inevitably turn towards expansion to seek funds, causing alarm in the market. The opening price fell to 57-58 yuan. After opening, banks tended to bargain, and a sudden surge of bargain hunters caused prices to rise, but there was still a further decline. Once the HSBC bank's exchange rate was known to be 0.125 higher for the British pound and 0.375 higher for the US dollar, the momentum waned, as the settlement price was still more than 50 yuan away. With banks bargain-hunting, the exchange rate tightened, and buying interest became more active, breaking through the 60 yuan mark and rising. A settlement of funds from the British American Tobacco company further tightened the domestic market, boosting sentiment and pushing gold prices higher. However, after two instances of supply at high prices, the upward trend stopped, and sentiment became uneasy again. In addition, due to the sharp overnight declines for several days, the supply in the market increased, but downstream demand was limited. However, because banks still had an appetite and buyers continued to maintain support, prices were still able to rise, but ultimately lacked the power to surge. Therefore, short sellers did not become active, and the market situation appeared uncertain. The yarn market remained difficult to boost. Although prices rose, they could not sustain, but the downward trend also lacked power. The morning market showed a pattern of fluctuating. Supplement to Shen Bao This City

Talks

Banning Inferior Private Schools

— OH

The pretext is "rectifying education," which no one dares to question and is undeniable!

However, we must admit that "the existence of a fact is never accidental." It has its own "social background"! Then, we cannot regard the "banning of private schools" as an isolated issue. At the very least, before banning private schools, we must first examine the reasons why private schools can exist in society, and then investigate them, so that it will not become a "stopgap"!

These two days, opening the newspaper is indeed dazzling, with recruitment ads everywhere. Some even use the tactics of commercial advertising, such as XX School's "few places left, register quickly," and other schools' beautiful sentences, such as "our school has fresh air and convenient transportation," "complete equipment," and so on, all of which are "luring customers," and are completely "commercialized"! As for the government-run schools? Although there are sometimes advertisements in the newspaper, stating when the school will enroll, but on the day of the exam, the required number can only be a fraction of the number of applicants. Of course, many students fail!

Where do these failed students go? That is the reason for the development of private schools. Many failed students, as long as they have the ability to study, have to enter a school (in the ordinary mentality, having attended a school means having received education, and it is also easier to find a job!). But the number of government-run places is limited, so they have to see those tempting advertisements in the newspapers and invest in that kind of school!

But, this is only part of the reason. At the same time, there is also a class of "people who use reading as a cover." In the minds of these people, reading is just a necessary procedure at the moment, and they will not rely on reading to eat in the future. Therefore, they don't need to pay attention to their studies. Fortunately, they only regard it as a cover. It seems a bit out of place if they don't read, and it doesn't sound good in society. Do these people go to strict schools? Too hard, not used to it. Therefore, "take off your pants to fart" type of private schools are very suitable for their taste.

However, "private schools" are not necessarily worse than "government-run" schools. Many "private schools" have more generous funding than "government-run" schools, but only a very small number. At the same time, the students in government-run schools are not all diligent students. In this modern age of deception, it is difficult to avoid it in the education field. There are some people with real talent and learning who cannot get into XX school, but those who have a nominal school status and know the school directors or the principal's relatives can enter with their heads held high, which prevents genuine students from "not being able to enter the door, or those who can enter are few," isn't it too unfair?

Finally, before the Ministry of Education bans inferior private schools, it is hoped that it can actively create several perfect schools. Otherwise, simply "banning" without "building" is not a good policy. No matter what, you must open a path for people to walk on before you can ban the path of inferior thorns! But construction is not a simple problem. If we want to build, we must build thoroughly, not construction that recycles old goods. The current banning of inferior private schools is only eliminating the bad ones, but simply destroying the bad ones is not enough. We must also build good schools! To build good schools, we must first concretely recognize society and reform it correctly. Otherwise, if education and society are irrelevant, it will lose the original purpose of running education.

Date After Dusk

— Chen Liang

The sun is still hanging high in the sky.

Li Da's heart is burning like fire. As soon as he finishes hoeing to the end of a field ridge, he raises his head to look at the sky, to look at the sun. His thoughts are also unsettled. As soon as he thinks of that round face and plump arms, his hands are so soft, and his eyes are so flowery, it's as if he has a charming girl like A Jin in front of him. He reaches out his hand, but damn it, he touches nothing.

He holds the rake in his hand, lazily hoeing, hoeing. The clods of dirt jump, and his heart also jumps. He raises his head again to look at the sun, that cumbersome thing that seems to be nailed to the sky. Usually, the daylight is very short, and the sun rolls down the mountain as soon as it comes out. Today, it's awkward and won't roll down for a long time. He feels like jumping into the sky to pick it down in a rage.

He really can't focus.

……"Wait for me in the cypress tree grave at dusk." Li Da remembers this sentence firmly, this sentence that was said with enthusiasm and a shy expression. This morning, he met A Jin by the oxcart shed. She only said one sentence to him, and her cheeks turned red, and the blood seemed to be about to spurt from her fingertips.

"Damn it, who can I talk to about my troubles?" At this time, Li Da only hopes that it will be night, only hopes that dusk will come quickly. He longs for the loveliness of dusk.

When he is lost in thought, he puts down the rake, sits on the mound, and stares blankly. Sometimes he says to himself in his heart: "I'm so old, and I haven't married a wife yet. Last year was a good year, and I was thinking of getting engaged, but the market outside is bad, and the imported rice and wheat have lowered the price of food. What with the winter defense donation, the security donation, and the highway fee, you have to spend money horizontally, and you have to spend money vertically. Looking at it, Li Da is bound to be a bachelor for life."

Being a bachelor for life is not just empty talk. There are many middle-aged men in the countryside who haven't married a wife. They don't have money. It's not easy to raise one child with this situation. But those with family wealth have several women, concubines. Damn it, shameless girls all run after those with money, eating oil, wearing silk, enjoying happiness, letting their bodies be swallowed by toads, being a dog to relieve boredom for others, spineless!

But, there are also those who are fierce.

Isn't that so? Take A Jin, she can be counted as one if she stretches out her fingers. She hasn't been caught by her cousin's hook several times. She doesn't love the shiny foreign money, she doesn't love eating well, she doesn't envy others' happiness. She has said:

"Cows in the countryside have to be slaughtered and used as food when they get to the city, and their milk is squeezed out to be used as a tonic for those with money. Girls are not much different from cows. Why think about the city? Isn't it good to live in the countryside? Do some work and eat, who says it's not good!"

When the sun rolls to the edge of the mountain hollow, Li Da jumps up from the mound. He remembers A Jin's unexpected deep affection for himself. His steps also become lighter. He carries the rake on his shoulder, returns home, washes his feet hastily, and eats two bowls of wheat porridge. His father tells him to twist hemp rope, but he ignores him and sneaks away.

He opens his eyes wide and squats alone in the cypress tree grave. Grains of starlight flicker in the village. The moon rolls into the sky from the west. In the distance, a black shadow is walking on the high levee, getting closer and closer.

"A Jin!"

"Who is A Jin, little devil, hiding and not doing anything good."

"Oh! Little Yinmei, I'll catch a firefly for you to play with."

"Do you think I care about you catching one?"……

Little Yinmei walks into the village. Li Da wipes away a handful of sweat and turns his gaze to the high levee again, waiting……

His heart is constantly chanting, "Dusk, oh! Dusk!"……

Common Ailments of Women

— Ben

Times have finally evolved. Chinese women, who have always been locked in their boudoirs, seem to be another kind of human species, having no opportunity to meet men in society and careers. Thus, a Daiyu-style of beauty has been formed. The fact tells us that in the past, Chinese women were for men to vent their lust, to pass on their genes, and nothing more. However, times have finally evolved. After the 1911 Revolution, Chinese women have raised the banner of confronting men. Year after year, after more than twenty years of shouting, women seem to have formed a lineup. Look, there are female committee members, female county magistrates, female secretaries, female adjutants, female police officers, which line doesn't have them?

Yes, this is a sign of the evolution of the times! This is the gospel of the evolution of women! The glory of the extension of women's rights! How worthy it is for us to praise!

However, regrettably, the fact is so distorted! Although there are female committee members, female county magistrates, etc., they are just a little embellishment in the long history, a kind of insignificant personal development, which has not established a role model for the entire women's community. In other words, most women today have not broken free from the old shackles of the past, but have only added a new layer of powder on the surface. Although it seems that there has been great progress, the bone marrow is still the same.

Strictly speaking, the current women's pathology, that is, the mistakes, is actually more serious than before. Just looking at the number of disputes caused by women, one can imagine the general situation. Such facts occupy large areas of newspapers every day, and they are all eye-catching. There is no need to list them in detail.

Let's analyze it and see.

(1) The Rising of Vanity丨丨In the past, Chinese women, although they were appendages of men, did not have much vanity. The so-called "marry a chicken follow a chicken, marry a dog follow a dog" is truly a vivid portrayal. They had nothing but to rely on heaven for food and to rely on heaven to arrange their lives. Now it's different. The most obvious is the rising of vanity. No matter what they do, they only seek the satisfaction of vanity, and they can ignore everything else. For example, during the study period, nine out of ten female students are slaves to grades, desperately fighting with teachers. As long as the grades are the highest, the actual knowledge is not in their mind. Participating in sports is also for the cheers of the audience. After leaving school, doing a wife must also ask whether there is family wealth and whether there is power. All of this is caused by vanity.

(2) The Preservation of Slave Mentality丨丨Although it is said that now it is equal between men and women, and men and women serve in society equally. However, because of the rising of their vanity, they are ultimately unable to open up an independent path and establish an independent personality. Therefore, we will not go into the period of studying or being in the boudoir. Once they graduate and marry a man, they fully reveal their slave mentality. They originally regarded marriage as a career, and they solved their material and spiritual lives through marriage. Therefore, the life of a modern woman ends as soon as she gets married. They only know how to act coquettishly and flatter in front of their husbands in order to win their favor. Everything else can be ignored. This kind of performance of slave mentality is really the only fatal injury to women's movement.

(3) The Desire for Enjoyment is Very Strong丨丨According to the first mistake, because vanity is very heavy, and they only know how to be "parasites," they can't talk about production themselves. Of course, they only know how to enjoy. It's okay to enjoy, but they also have a very strong desire, blindly rushing towards the "happiness" side, fully exposing the symptoms of women. If this continues, how can they not fall into a trap and be trampled on? How can they not also ruin their own personality? Destroy the development of women's movement?

Women, the times tell us that this is definitely not your way out. Wake up!

Night Scene on the Huangpu River

— Fei

The curtain of night has already descended upon the world: the late summer evening breeze has brought a gentle coolness. The electric street lamps suddenly shine brightly, and the neon lights spew out their red flames. It is as if a golden serpent of ten thousand rays of light is dancing in the air, illuminating the street corners as if it were daytime. People and cars are interwoven in the streets, women holding onto men, men chasing after women, surging,澎湃, and激盪 in the roads like an angry tide.

Beside the Huangpu River, the great bell of the Jianghai Customs House stands tall in the sky: it seems not to feel the dreadfulness of the summer sun or the winter northwest wind! It diligently performs its duty of telling time day and night. The god of peace stands alone by the river, shedding tears!

Along the road, scattered among the trees, are dotted dim lights: the river breeze strikes people's faces, bringing a slight warmth. Every tram is packed full, and the convertibles are running at full throttle, racing each other on the road like flying. The docks of the city ferries are crowded with people, men and women; the sound of coins at the ticket booths jingles. "Toot! Toot!" With two blasts of the whistle, the ship leaves the dock, taking a boatload of people enjoying the cool lake breeze, rushing towards Wusong against the waves. A crowd of people is left behind, forced to stare enviously as it gradually disappears into the starry, misty waves.

The evening tide rises into the Huangpu River, the waves striking the shore, emitting a clear crashing sound, like the weeping of women or the groaning of patients; so bleak, so cold!

Looking across the river, the scattered lights are truly as beautiful and serene as the stars in the night sky. However, some shadows of constructions are faintly visible, the only aggressive weapons of a few imperialists! Warships! Standing silently in the heart of the river.

On the lawn by the river, many toiling masses, driven out of their houses by the heat, lie in rows like wounded soldiers after a defeat. In their eyes, perhaps, this is a summer resort just like Lushan or Moganshan.

Groups of people flow into the gate of the Bund Park: there is no longer a single empty spot on the chairs or the grass. Under the shelter of the trees, couples are cuddling and embracing: in the center of the park,藤 tables and chairs selling cold drinks are full. The radio plays exotic tunes. Sailors with loose morals, arm in arm with "salty water girls," stagger through the pedestrians, humming lion-like tunes, a strange-smelling alcoholic stench making people want to vomit. People avoid them from afar, but their greedy eyes are fixed on the beautiful Chinese women.

On the grass, in the shadows of the lights, lay stretched out | quite a few people, each with a woman sitting beside them, whispering something?

There are also many small comedies of romance being played out there, perhaps, I conjecture.

A crescent moon, incomplete and not perfectly round, shyly reveals a face like a virgin from the horizon, gradually rising into the sky, scattering ten thousand rays of silver light, illuminating the turbid Huangpu River as if it were filled with mercury. Beautiful ripples, swaying with the wind, the clear brilliance, permeate everyone's heart, arousing boundless, unimaginable fantasies.

Random Thoughts

— Bing

Foreword

The three characters (天曉得) "Tian Xiao De" [God Knows] have long been a commonplace expression in the mouths of Chinese people. Its meaning is very clear, but its origin is untraceable. My friend (?) Hu Shi is far away in Beiping; otherwise, I would have called on him to humbly ask him about it, and writing about it would have been "精" (refined) and "采" (brilliant), much more valuable. But the topic has been set, and the goods must be delivered to paper. I cannot wait, so I can only talk about it "朦朧" (vaguely). Fortunately, its meaning is clear, and readers are mostly wise, so it is not difficult to understand. "Tian Xiao De" is similar to "莫明其妙" [inexplicable]. This is considered the foreword.

Yesterday, colleague X, who is in charge of academic affairs, said to me: "The level of the students here is truly laughable. A high school graduate came to collect his certificate, and when I handed it over, I asked him to provide a simple receipt. He actually said he didn't know how to write it and asked me to do it for him..."

On the other hand, since the summer vacation, most of the graduates from various schools in Beiping have had no way out, so they initiated a career movement, followed by Nanjing Zhongda and this local Jinda. I have paid special attention to the occurrence of this movement from the beginning. It still seems to be just a lot of shouting with no results. University graduates are not easily cultivated? Logically, they should be the most useful and highest-level talents, but in fact, they are busy shouting about finding a way out, which is truly bewildering and maddening to see.

The performance of this matter is a general liquidation of the bankruptcy of Chinese education, and it is also a sign that society has reached an extreme state of decline. Apart from repeatedly calling out "Tian Xiao De," I really have nothing else to say.

There are especially many things worth noting in Shanghai society, especially in such a hot season. Every morning, when I open the newspaper and look at the social news section, I always find one or two shocking miracles. To put it bluntly, if you go to the streets for sightseeing, you will constantly see things that will break your heart. If you don't believe me, listen to what I have to say:

In the evening, the girls from poor families escape the sweltering attics or small rooms, thinking of going to the alley entrance to breathe in some cooler air. They shouldn't have to worry about the precept of "a son of a thousand gold does not sit under a leaning eaves," but even then, unexpected disasters can fly in from nowhere. There are some wretched people who don't care if your age is only five or six years old, let alone whether you are fully grown. As long as they have the opportunity 丨丨 no one is around, and they see you alone, they will look to you for a place to vent their sexual urges. Thus, the news of the rape of a X-year-old girl and the conviction is produced.

On hot days, the cold drink business is ten times more profitable. Ice cream, shaved ice, all kinds of soda, one bottle after another is sent to the mouths of the rich. But on the streets, there are many coolies picking up watermelon rinds (please note, really watermelon rinds!) that others have eaten and discarded on the ground, biting them piece by piece, as if the coolness is refreshing and can fill their stomachs, with endless flavor. Sometimes, three or five of them are fighting over them, causing a big commotion.

Rickshaw pullers, bare-shouldered and barefoot, are willing to pull people at low prices under the fiery sun to earn a living. The people in the rickshaws, wearing cicada-wing-like silk and gauze clothes, holding umbrellas above their heads, and waving fans in their hands, "Hot, hot, the third one is deadly hot," quietly and elegantly comes out of their mouths.

In the Zhabei Dayang Bridge Tanzhiwan area, after nightfall, it is like a "nudist colony." Children, needless to say, are all stark naked, and even adult men and women are mostly unclothed. The roadside is their natural large bed. As a result, diseases occur frequently, and no one has money to deal with them, so deaths follow one after another, but the wealthy turn a deaf ear.

These, these, are all considered "Tian Xiao De."

Random Words During Illness

— Ding

It is painful when a person is heartbroken, it is painful when a person is frustrated, it is painful in a life environment that is neither alive nor dead, it is painful when a person is sick, and it is even more painful when a person is sick alone and has no friends, relatives, or loved ones to take care of and comfort them; this pain is deeply engraved in my mind, in my heart, in the flow of my blood!

This pain is a kind of helpless and unsupported pain, a kind of cruel pain, a kind of great pain without emotion! From these pains, I have experienced many lessons and the essence of life. From these pains, I have learned many valuable ways of being a person!

For my own lonely sorrow, I once stirred up a thread of sadness. In the silent night, I used my weak elbow to support my head, which was causing mental pain due to anxious thinking. Under the dim light of the lamp in the room, I held a sorrowful mood and, with a tragic attitude, gazed out with my tearful eyes. Outside the window, it was also dim, bleak, and dull, a gray night! As if it were the same as my mood.

Although the sky was full of stars, accompanied by a crescent moon like an eyebrow, this scenery, not only would not arouse my admiration, but, for a person who is being entangled by illness and fighting against loneliness, how unfortunate this is!

The change in a person's consciousness caused by the pain of illness is terrible, dangerous, and may even lead me to a path of destruction in helplessness!

At this time, a thought of suicide suddenly surged in my heart. I felt that it was better to die than to suffer this unbearable pain for living in vain! Isn't death the end of all suffering?

Is it absolutely unacceptable to wait for death with eyes wide open, to let the disease arbitrarily go wild on one's body, trampling and ravaging it? Although my body cannot resist it at this time, my spirit must fight it desperately.

Death is absolutely unavoidable. Yes, I would rather end my life quickly. After all, there is no good in living like that.

I feel that I don't need people's help anymore. Because I understand that behind the assistance lies a kind of despicable attempt. Therefore, it is better not to seek help from anyone!

As for pity, it is an insult to me, I do not accept anyone's pity. Sincere comfort is certainly a noble sympathy, but this sympathy is not easily revealed. But those false exhortations, fake enthusiasm, perfunctory attitude, I plug my ears, close my eyes, I hate those hypocritical guys!

In illness, I truly understand the truth and falsehood of friends and feelings, the happiness of health, and the taste of pain.

In illness, I have experienced people's deception, people's indifference, people's cruelty, human selfishness, human violence, human meanness, human wildness...

In illness, I feel how boring and base humans are! Allowing pain and disaster to eat away at a life that could be saved, this cannot but be said to be human unreasonableness and brutality.

Amateur Mailbox

Temperament Change

— Editor

Dear Editor!

I have a friend who told me about something difficult and needs to solve, but with my limited knowledge, how can I solve this difficult thing! So I ask for your help.

This friend of mine is now 23 years old. When he was fifteen years old, he gave up school to work. Because of his good character and careful work, he was appreciated by his teacher. After two years of observation, in 1928, he was introduced by his teacher to get engaged. The girl he is engaged to is the daughter of his teacher's wife's sister. The two sides often interact, and everyone is familiar. This girl often goes to their house, sometimes staying overnight or for a few days. In this transitional era, this marriage is very good, but recently, according to my friend, this girl has disappointed him very much. I asked him, how do you know? He said: "During the January 28th Shanghai Incident, she stayed in my house for several days. Because we lived together every day, it was easy to observe her. Her temper is extremely bad, she is very stingy and not generous! She is also lazy by nature and does not know how to cherish herself. My family also despises her (because she has done indecent things). If I marry her, not only will there be no love, but the relationship between the two sides will be bad. What's the point? And the family relationship will also break down, so my friend is very worried and spends his days in a city of sorrow. Now, I would like to propose two questions and ask you to answer them: 1. If he doesn't want to marry her, of course, he will break the engagement. What steps should he take? What methods are needed? What if she doesn't want to? 2. If he doesn't break the engagement with her, what methods can he take to change her temper and make her a good person? The above two questions urgently need your help to solve them. Wishing you good health. Sincerely,

Answer: Since your friend now has such a bad impression of the other party, it is of course better to break the engagement. The method of breaking the engagement is very simple: he can directly express it to the other party, or have the original matchmaker convey his intention to break the engagement. Now the effect of marriage contracts is very weak. If his will is very firm, the other party cannot force him, but the other party can ask him for compensation for damages. The second point, what methods can be used to make her temper better, this question is very difficult to answer. Because a person's temperament and character are not necessarily innate, but mainly cultivated by the environment, but once cultivated, it is very difficult to reform. As the saying goes, "It is easy to change mountains and rivers, but difficult to change one's nature." But temper is not impossible to change, and a person is not unable to become "good." In my opinion, your friend's fiancée's bad temper and character are probably due to poor education and lack of knowledge. Therefore, if he wants to hope that she becomes a "good person," he may as well start with education and try.

Fiction

The Idiot (2)

— Lin Bin

The children surrounded him, playing with him like playing with a monkey in a monkey show troupe: some picked up stones from the roadside and threw them at him: some used the roasted beans their mothers gave them to tease him: several children whose fathers owned small sundries shops took out slippery dried jujube pits from their mouths and hit him. They stamped their small feet, hummed with their small mouths, made gestures, and chanted in unison, issuing sarcasm like raindrops in a heavy rain:

"Idiot, do you want a wife?"

"Do you want a细毛相的 (fine-haired) girl, idiot?"

"Plum blossom pattern, bamboo tube legs, so beautiful! Do you want it?"

His round face, floating with the helpless sorrow of the oppressed, immediately flashed with a glimmer of hope, and he uttered a semi-believing echo from between his thick, clumsy lips:

"Of course I want a wife. Really? Where is she? Take me to see her, go, go!"

The children laughed so hard they couldn't catch their breath, bending over as if they had a stomachache.

"Here, it's him! Take it to the wedding!" pointing to a dog by the roadside.

Then disappointment, sorrow, and anger intertwined on his hairy face, and his lips moved constantly, obviously chewing on the taste of "bitterness."

However, just as all idiots who are accustomed to being trampled on and played with sometimes force smart people to temporarily hide their fierce faces behind gentle and amiable smiles, hidden in small favors like arsenic pills wrapped in white sugar, and that is for the purpose of trampling on them and playing with them even more cruelly. Our idiot also has times when he is seemingly fragrant on the surface, times when he can obtain food that he cannot beg for without having to beg, and times when children dare not play with him under the reprimands of adults, but the price he pays for accepting this unconventional treatment is naturally not just a few non-itchy, non-painful scoldings and laughter, or even a few small slaps that only give a momentary small pain.

Whenever the sky hangs with a misty rain net, and small puddles are dotted on the road, all the women who have no men, or whose men cannot carry water or are lazy to carry water in the rain, think of the idiot in unison. They first scrape their respective water tanks clean, and some,嫌 (disliking) that the water tanks are too small, also prepare an empty tank. Then they lean on the楼 (multi-storied) windows facing the street, or stand upright at the gate, listening intently to the idiot's call, like waiting for honored guests who bring 声香 (prestige and fortune).

Supplement to the Shanghai Shenbao - Film Special

On Anti-War Films and Their Stance

— Danfeng

If we are not blind, if we do not want to be submissive people of imperialism, the current frenzy of imperialist war preparations has reached a point of madness, and we should not dare to ignore it.

Regarding the facts of this matter, there are almost countless examples. The US Navy's joint maneuvers in the Pacific and Atlantic, Britain's desperate expansion of its navy, France's unprecedented increase in military spending, Italy's construction of many warships of more than 30,000 tons and the distant expeditions of aircraft with iron wings covering the sky, Germany's Hitler's insistence on military equality and the expansion of his secret infantry, Japan's active invasion of North China and its constant challenges to the Soviet Union... Are these facts not enough to illustrate the mad war preparations of imperialism?

Recently, due to the death of Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss, the sharp opposition between the Versailles system and the anti-Versailles system has further become a direct conflict. Italy has even threatened to intervene with force, and France has disapproved of Papen as ambassador to Austria. Such facts show that the outbreak of war is possible at any time.

On the other hand, due to the rapid advancement of socialist construction in the Soviet Union, contrasted with the European and American countries' transition from relative stability after the war to the final stage of collapse, the doors of war and revolution are approaching: the opposition between the two worlds has promoted the active offensive against the Soviet Union by the East and the West. Britain has replaced France as the organizer of Poland, Romania, and other vassal states. The German Foreign Minister publicly declared the division of the Soviet Union. Japan's active espionage war on the northeastern border indicates the active growth of a new crusade. But until now, no military action has been launched. On the one hand, it is indeed because the fundamental contradictions between imperialists are difficult to eliminate, and on the other hand, the internal unrest of various countries and the growth of revolutionary forces are also the main reasons. Now it is a new cycle of war and revolution. It is an inevitable trend to eliminate imperialist war with revolutionary war.

Then, in this night of storms, what is reflected in the films? In Germany, in Japan, in Italy, because Fascism itself is the cause of war, we see that they are using films to organize war and welcome war. Similarly, in the United States, it is no exception. From many newsreels and from many films with war as the subject matter, we can even see the filmmakers' fanaticism for war.

However, in order to uphold world peace, especially in semi-colonial China, in order not to let China become the battlefield of the Second World War, in order to ensure that we do not die under poisonous gas bombs and become cannon fodder for imperialism, we must use all our strength to oppose the great war. Therefore, we must fulfill our mission in the film and produce anti-war films.

Naturally, what we require is not only anti-war films with a humanitarian aversion to war, but also a further step. We must correctly analyze the nature of the great war and explain the causes and consequences of the imperialist war. Moreover, in China, the production of anti-war films must not conflict with the launch of anti-imperialist and anti-Japanese films. We oppose imperialist wars, but we must have a large number of films that organize anti-imperialist and anti-Japanese national revolutionary wars. To be precise, only by launching a national war can we eliminate imperialist war and achieve a victorious future for China.

Film Review

Review of "It Happened One Night"

— Ling He

Ｈeads　We　Go！丨Cathay

The so-called twists and turns of the plot occupy a very important position in the beliefs of European and American filmmakers, which is an undeniable fact. Because of this, screenwriters have to open their minds to create some bizarre stories, and the question of whether they make sense is something they don't have to worry about.

"It Happened One Night" is a film that was reluctantly made under such circumstances. The irrationality of the plot is not only that the young woman Pei Di impersonates the star Tao Leshan Kai because of her similar appearance, which we dare not believe, but also that when the agent of the real Tao Leshan Kai encounters the fake Tao Lesai Kai on the cruise, he only needs to announce it publicly and the secret will be revealed immediately. And it is also unlikely that the young master will dress up as a waiter or ticket inspector.

Since the story is so illogical, then it is obvious that it does not represent reality. And how do the playwrights serve their class in the middle of this? Pei Di, a young lady from a modest family, meets a young master by chance, and they immediately fall in love within three minutes. And under the theme of instigating them to climb up, she is unhappy when she sees him turn into a waiter, but she suddenly becomes happy when he turns into the host of a feast on a cruise, and she is surprised again when he turns into a ticket inspector on the train. In the end, she finally realizes that he is indeed the son of a news tycoon, so she and he truly (?) fall in love. 丨丨The whole thing is a distorted and clumsy sermon.

Of course, with such a script, no matter how clever the director is, there will be no good results, let alone that the director Monty Banks cannot achieve a certain degree of success in form very cleverly. Compared to the director Frank Capra of "One Night of Passion," who can act as a liar and make people almost believe the absurd story, the director of "It Happened One Night" is far behind.

Perhaps it can be said that there is nothing terribly wrong here. He always fulfills his responsibilities based on the illogical story, but some scenes are filmed as silent films and then dubbed with music, and even the applause that should be on the screen or the voices of people talking in the dance hall are gone. Secondly, the pretentious gags are also annoying to us.

The actress Constance Bennett's acting skills are not very good, although she plays two roles at the same time and grasps the two personalities.

The rest are all average.

"Judging People by Appearances Lost Ziyu" Helen Hayes's Debut

— Xin Zhi

In the past, movie stars relied on "beauty salons" for survival. But in today's film industry, beauty of appearance is no longer so rare. More important than beauty of appearance are voice and expression. This is probably a change brought about by the transition from silent films to sound films.

Looking at today's general big stars, with a few exceptions, they are not very beautiful. Not only are their faces ordinary, but many are even below ordinary. However, they possess lively and stylish postures, enough to be a modern star.

Helen Hayes is a pioneer among this type of actor. She does not have beautiful looks. She has also never studied embellishment. She succeeded as a modern big star entirely because she has superb artistic skills.

When Helen Hayes first arrived in Hollywood, after several auditions, the directors and cameramen, seeing her thin face and dull eyes, did not get any impression of female beauty. Her first film was stopped after only half of it was shot. She went through several attempts to join companies, all ending in failure. Finally, she switched to MGM. When she was auditioning at the MGM studio, the director and cameraman secretly shook their heads.

"She's probably going to scare away the audience in the theater." MGM's general manager, Irving Thalberg, said to chief director Edgar Selwyn. Selwyn quietly looked at her for a long time, feeling that she lacked a glamorous appearance and was not suitable as a film actor. So he suggested to Thalberg to try her out again at his home.

After Selwyn set up an audition room, he said to Thalberg, "Please close your eyes and listen to her audition with your ears." Thalberg closed his eyes, and he listened quietly to Helen's audition, which had already begun. Her dialogue, trembling voice, and emotionally moving tone, as well as many touching endings, made people's minds stir.

Thalberg opened his eyes, and tears had dripped from his eyes. He looked at Helen, forgetting her ordinary appearance, and felt that she was a very touching woman. From then on, Helen was chosen as a rare talent and became the protagonist of many famous films. The Academy Award from the Academy of Motion Picture Arts and Sciences in 1932 also went to her. Her face is not beautiful, but her status is extremely high!

A Collection of New Information about "The Good Earth"

— Huang Yingdai

Regarding director Hale's remarks after "The Good Earth" photography team returned to the United States, this publication has already reported to readers. What is reported here are some other new news about "The Good Earth."

Although it has been several weeks since "The Good Earth" photography team left China and returned to the United States, the two issues of actors and dialogue have not been resolved until now.

Although director George Hale shot a lot of location shots in China, the list of actors has not been finalized until now. He has already examined Chinese actresses and American stars on the spot, but for several weeks, this problem has not been solved.

American movie fans unanimously say that Chinese people cannot express the emotions of the characters in the play on the screen, but Hale saw the expressions of Chinese actors on the screen in China, including what he examined, and has completely expressed that this statement is incorrect. At the same time, he recalled that Ramon Novarro and Helen Hayes came to the East to shoot the film "Son-Daughter" and were not very satisfied.

But from another perspective, many male and female Hollywood stars have had considerable success in performing Eastern roles in the past, such as Richard Barthelmess in "Broken Blossoms," Edward G. Robinson in "The Hatchet Man," Warner Oland and Nils Asther have also played the same roles, in addition to Rudolph Valentino, Myrna Loy, and Helen Hayes have also played oriental women, these are Westerners performing oriental roles.

Regarding the dialogue, some people feel that the production technique of "Eskimo", using a native language with English subtitles, can be completely applied to "The Good Earth" for comparison, and it is much more appropriate to use English completely, although there are various difficulties.

In order to solve the above two problems, it is now being considered to use two kinds of dialogue. One is English and the other is Chinese. In the future, Chinese will be used when it is released in the East, and English will be used in the West. As for the actors, there will also be two teams, Chinese and Americans, each filming one film.

Film Novel

Good Son, Good Wife (Born to be Kissed) (11)

— Xin Zhi

After Tom left, Mr. Pan was still standing still, his mind full of thoughts. After a while, he walked to the door of the large restaurant and carried his secretary, Miss Newbright, out. He ordered her to find the local prosecutor. Miss Newbright was startled when she heard this and quickly asked what was wrong. Pan Qidao said, "There is a small problem. That delusional woman has colluded with my son, and I want to find a way to deal with her." What method did he use? Only his cunning mind could think of it. At this time, Tom had already returned to the small apartment where Eddie and Kitty lived together. They were in high spirits, unaware that a trap had been set up, waiting to catch a turtle in a jar. At first, Eddie didn't quite believe it. But Tom told her, "My father and I have already made it clear. He just wants me to be happy, and he can do anything." He also told her everything about his conversation with his father, and she finally believed it. Tom even called her Mrs. Tom Panqi, which made Eddie's heart beat faster with happiness. She said, "I also want to do many things: I want to hire a teacher to re-teach my English... I also want to study some French... I will no longer use lemon juice to wash my hair in the future..." Tom didn't wait for her to continue, and sealed her words with a kiss on her lips. After a while, she said again, "My clothes, I will try to keep them simple in the future... Like those friends of yours in Palm Beach... Can we two always be together at first?" Tom called her, "Baby, of course you can. Don't worry." After he said that, he told her that he had to go back to his father's party. He said, "This is the last time I'm going alone. I'll call you first thing tomorrow. I'll have the pastor take care of everything for us." Eddie hugged his hand as if she was still a little scared and asked, "Tom, is everything real?" Tom kissed her again and comforted her, "Sweetheart, don't worry. Everything is real. Go to sleep well, tomorrow will be a hard day."

After Tom left, Eddie happily took off her clothes and sat on the bed. Kitty and a sailor went out to play. Eddie was so happy that she wanted to sit and wait for Kitty to come back and tell her all the good news. Suddenly, someone knocked on the door outside. Eddie quickly put on a coat and got out of bed to ask who it was. No one answered outside, so she opened the door a crack to take a look. Unexpectedly, a man's foot had already stretched in. He pushed the door open. He ran in, closed the door again, and turned the key to lock the door. He then took off his upper body clothes. Eddie was so scared that she screamed, but the man just looked at her and smiled. After a while, someone knocked on the door again and knocked very urgently. The man went to open the door. As soon as the door opened, a policeman stood outside, followed by another. The policeman in front said, "We want to see Miss Eddie." The man who came in first put his hand on Eddie's shoulder and said, "Do you have official business?" Eddie inexplicably pushed the man's hand away, but the man hugged her and said, "Sweetheart, don't be afraid, I'm here." Eddie shouted at the police, "Who is this person? I don't know him!" But the policeman just smiled and didn't answer, and moved aside. A photographer came up from behind and took a picture of them... Eddie was wearing a nightgown, and the strange man was only wearing a shirt, and his arm was on Eddie's shoulder! After the photographer took the picture, he mischievously said, "This is great, thank you both." Then the police officer strode to Eddie and shouted, "Put on your clothes. Come with us!" They took Eddie away. (To be continued)
